when you say she's a programmer , she did do some , but the real thing is to have said the future is going to be much , much more than this .	當你說她是個程式師 , 她做了一些 , 但真正的重點是要說未來將會比這樣的 。
now , a hundred years later , this guy comes along , alan turing , and in 1936 , and invents the computer all over again .	現在 , 一百年後 , 這個傢伙來到1936年 , 發明了電腦 。
now , of course , babbage's machine was entirely mechanical .	當然 , 巴比的機器是完全機械 。
turing's machine was entirely theoretical .	turing是完全合理的 。
both of these guys were coming from a mathematical perspective , but turing told us something very important .	這些傢伙都從數學角度來看 , 但要告訴我們一些非常重要的事 。
he laid down the mathematical foundations for computer science , and said , " it doesn't matter how you make a computer . "	他說: 「 電腦科學基礎基礎基礎基礎基礎基礎建設電腦科學基礎 。 」
it doesn't matter if your computer's mechanical , like babbage's was , or electronic , like computers are today , or perhaps in the future , cells , or , again , mechanical again , once we get into nanotechnology .	不管你電腦的機械 , 比如巴比的機械 , 如今電腦一樣 , 或電子 , 或在未來 , 再次 , 再次 , 再次我們進入奈米學 。
we could go back to babbage's machine and just make it tiny . all those things are computers .	我們可以回到babbage的機器 , 讓它微小 。 所有這些東西都是電腦 。
there is in a sense a computing essence .	在某種程度上 , 有一個計算機 。
this is called the church–turing thesis .	這叫做教堂教堂 ,
and so suddenly , you get this link where you say this thing babbage had built really was a computer .	所以突然間 , 你得到了這張圖書館 , 你說這張圖是電腦的 。
in fact , it was capable of doing everything we do today with computers , only really slowly .	事實上 , 我們今天能用電腦做所有事 , 只能慢地慢地做所有事 , 真的很慢 。
to give you an idea of how slowly , it had about 1k of memory .	為了給各位一個想法如何慢慢地 , 它有大約一公分之一 。
it used punch cards , which were being fed in , and it ran about 10 , 000 times slower the first zx81 .	它使用了一萬倍的車子 , 它很奇怪 , 大約有10萬倍 。
it did have a ram pack .	它有一個種族攻擊 。
you could add on a lot of extra memory if you wanted to .	你可以在很多外交記憶中加上很多 。
so , where does that bring us today ?	那麼 , 這帶給我們什麼 ?
so there are plans .	所以有植物 。
over in swindon , the science museum archives , there are hundreds of plans and thousands of pages of notes written by charles babbage about this analytical engine .	在瑞典博物館裡 , 科學博物館裡有數百種植物和數千個小型的小小小部分 , 關於這個分析的工程程 。
one of those is a set of plans that we call plan 28 , and that is also the name of a charity that i started with doron swade , who was the curator of computing at the science museum , and also the person who drove the project to build a difference engine , and our plan is to build it .	這是我們稱之為計劃28歲的植物之一 , 這也是我從科學博物館的名字 , 他是從科學博物館的曲線 , 也是為了建造不同的工程師 , 我們的計畫是建造一個不同工程師 , 我們的計畫就是建造它 。
here in south kensington , we will build the analytical engine .	在南韓 , 我們會建造一個分析工程程 。
the project has a number of parts to it .	這項計畫有許多部分 。
one was the scanning of babbage's archive .	一個是babbage的掃描 。
that's been done . the second is now the study of all of those plans to determine what to build .	第二個計畫已經完成了 。 現在第二個計畫來決定建造什麼 。
the third part is a computer simulation of that machine , and the last part is to physically build it at the science museum .	第三個部分是電腦模擬博物館 , 最後一部分是物理博物館 。
when it's built , you'll finally be able to understand how a computer works , because rather than having a tiny chip in front of you , you've got to look at this humongous thing and say , " ah , i see the memory operating , i see the cpu operating , i hear it operating . i probably smell it operating . "	當它建構時 , 你終於能夠了解電腦運作 , 因為不是有小小的晶片 , 而是在你面前 , 你必須仔細觀察這個奇怪的事情 , 我看到了這個巨大的事情 , 我看到了它的記憶 。 」
but in between that we're going to do a simulation .	但在於我們要做一個模擬 。
babbage himself wrote , he said , as soon as the analytical engine exists , it will surely guide the future course of science .	babbage寫英雄 , 他說 , 身為分析工程程存在 , 它一定會引導科學的未來 。
of course , he never built it , because he was always fiddling with new plans , but when it did get built , of course , in the 1940s , everything changed .	當然 , 他從來沒有建構它 , 因為他總是用新的計劃 , 但在1940年代 , 一切都改變了 。
now , i'll just give you a little taste of what it looks like in motion with a video which shows just one part of the cpu mechanism working .	現在 , 我要給各位一點一點一點一點點 , 它看起來像是在動機系統工作的一部分之一 , 顯示一部分清潔機制之一 。
so this is just three sets of cogs , and it's going to add . this is the adding mechanism in action , so you imagine this gigantic machine .	所以這只是三組認知機制 , 它會加入行動 , 所以你想像這個巨大的機制 , 所以你想像一下這個巨大機器 。
so , give me five years .	所以 , 給我五年 。
before the 2030s happen , we'll have it .	在2030年發生之前 , 我們將會有它 。
thank you very much .	謝謝大家 。

in this accessible talk from tedxboston , richard resnick shows how cheap and fast genome sequencing is about to turn health care upside down .	在tedxboton、richardrenick顯示出如何便宜和快速基因組序列的基因組 , 就是要把健康照護轉移到 。
dna , biotech , health care , science , technology	dna、健康照護、健康照護、科學、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、
richard resnick: welcome to the genomic revolution	理查尼克:歡迎到基因革命 。
ladies and gentlemen , i present to you the human genome .	女士們 , 我向各位介紹人類基因組 。
chromosome one , top left .	染色體第一 , 左邊 。
bottom right are the sex chromosomes .	底部是性染色體染色體
women have two copies of that big x chromosome ; men have the x and , of course , that small copy of the y .	女性有兩份大型x染色體 , 當然 , 男人有x和x , 當然 , 這小小的複製 。
sorry boys , but it's just a tiny little thing that makes you different .	抱歉男孩 , 但這只是個小東西讓你不同 。
so if you zoom in on this genome , then what you see , of course , is this double helix structure the code of life spelled out with these four biochemical letters , or we call them bases , right: a , c , g and t .	所以 , 如果你在這個基因組裡 , 那麼你會看到的 , 當然 , 這雙雙胞胎結構的編碼碼碼碼碼碼碼 , 或者我們稱它們為蝙蝠 , 或我們稱它們為蝙蝠、g和t 。
how many are there in the human genome ? three billion .	有多少人基因組中有多少 ?
is that a big number ?	那是個大數字嗎 ?
well , everybody can throw around big numbers .	嗯 , 每個人都可以在大數字上瀏覽 。
but in fact , if i were to place one base on each pixel of this 1280 by 800 resolution screen , we would need 3 , 000 screens to take a look at the genome .	但事實上 , 如果我要把這12800次的電池螢幕上 , 我們需要3千個螢幕 , 我們需要3千個螢幕來看看基因組 。
so it's really quite big .	所以這真的很大 。

so i'm thinking , you know , this procedure hasn't changed in about 40 years .	所以我想 , 你知道嗎 , 這個成功並沒有改變了大約40年 。
and there is probably a better way to do this .	可能有更好的方法 。
so i thought of a minimally invasive approach , and a new device that we call the marrow miner .	所以我想到一個最小的方法 , 而一個新的裝置 , 我們稱之為 「 箭頭 」 的新裝置 。
and the marrow miner , the way it works is shown here .	而火星礦礦工 , 它的運作方式是展示的 。
our standard seethrough patient .	我們的標準看病人 。
instead of entering the bone dozens of times , we enter just once , into the front of the hip or the back of the hip .	我們不是進入骨骼的骨頭 , 我們一旦進入山丘或背部的前面 , 進入山丘或背後的背景 。
and we have a flexible , powered catheter with a special wire loop tip that stays inside the crunchy part of the marrow and follows the contours of the hip , as it moves around .	我們有一個很棒的 , 強力的營運 , 用一個特殊的野生迴圈 , 遵循了火星的一部分 , 隨著它移動到山丘裡移動 。
so it enables you to very rapidly aspirate , or suck out , rich bone marrow very quickly through one hole .	所以 , 很快地讓你非常幸運 , 或是很幸運的骨髓 , 豐富骨髓很快地通過一個洞穴 。
we can do multiple passes through that same entry .	我們可以透過同樣的句子來操作 。
and , so , very quickly , bob can just get one puncture , local anesthesia , and do this harvest as an outpatient .	所以 , 很快地 , 鮑勃可以得到一個懲罰 , 當地的麻醉 , 當地的麻醉劑 。
so i did a few prototypes . i got a small little grant at stanford .	所以我做了幾張攝影機 。 我在史丹佛大學 。
and played around with this a little bit .	玩這個小一點 。
and our team members developed this technology .	我們的團隊成員開發了這項技術 。
and eventually we got two large animals , and pig studies .	最終 , 我們有兩個大動物 , 豬的研究 。
and we found , to our surprise , that we not only got bone marrow out , but we got 10 times the stem cell activity in the marrow from the marrow miner , compared to the normal device .	我們發現 , 為了我們的驚訝 , 我們不僅僅有骨髓活動 , 我們有10倍的幹細胞活動活動 , 我們收集了10倍的幹細胞活動 。
this device was just fda approved in the last year .	這裝置只是在過去一年的一年裡 。
here is a live patient . you can see it following the flexible curves around .	這是個肝臟病患 , 你可以看到它追蹤了飛行器 。
there will be two passes here , in the same patient , from the same hole .	在同一個洞穴裡 , 同一個洞穴的病人 , 從同樣的洞穴 。
this was done under local anesthesia , as an outpatient .	這是當地的麻醉劑 , 身為一個外科醫生 。
and we got , again , about three to six times more stem cells than the standard approach done on the same patient .	我們又再一次 , 大約有三到六倍的幹細胞比標準的方法 。
so why should you care ? bone marrow is a very rich source of adult stem cells .	所以 , 你為什麼要照顧 ? 骨髓是一個非常豐富的幹細胞 。
you all know about embryonic stem cells .	你知道胚胎幹細胞 。
they've got great potential but haven't yet entered clinical trials .	他們有很好的潛力 , 但沒有進入臨床試驗 。
adult stem cells are throughout our body , including the bloodforming stem cells in our bone marrow , which we've been using as a form of stemcell therapy for over 40 years .	成人的幹細胞在我們的骨髓中 , 包括血液的幹細胞 , 包括我們骨髓的幹細胞 。
in the last decade there's been an explosion of use of bone marrow stem cells to treat the patient's other diseases such as heart disease , vascular disease , orthopedics , tissue engineering , even in neurology to treat parkinson's and diabetes .	在過去十年間 , 使用骨髓幹細胞 , 用來治療病人的其他疾病 , 例如心臟疾病、血液疾病、疾病、血液、血液、組織工程、組織工程、糖尿病、糖尿病、糖尿病 。
we've just come out , we're commercializing , this year , generation 2 . 0 of the marrow miner .	我們剛剛出去 , 我們今年商業化了 , 世代2.0.0.0.0.0.0.0.
the hope is that this gets more stem cells out , which translates to better outcomes .	希望的是 , 這個希望讓更多幹細胞變得更好的結果 。
it may encourage more people to sign up to be potential livesaving bone marrow donors .	可能鼓勵更多人去簽署更多人去簽署骨髓捐贈者 。
it may even enable you to bank your own marrow stem cells , when you're younger and healthier , to use in the future should you need it .	甚至可能你要銀行自己的火星幹細胞 , 當你年輕、更健康、更健康、更健康、更健康 , 用在未來需要它 。
and ultimately and here's a picture of our bone marrow transplant survivors , who come together for a reunion each year at stanford .	最終 , 這是我們骨髓移植手術的照片 , 每年都聚在一起 , 他們聚集在一起 , 他們聚集在一起 。
hopefully this technology will let us have more of these survivors in the future .	希望這科技會讓我們有更多的倖存者 。
physicist and surfer garrett lisi presents a controversial new model of the universe that just maybe answers all the big questions . if nothing else , it's the most beautiful 8dimensional model of elementary particles and forces you've ever seen .	物理學家和urfergarretsgarret展示了一個宇宙模型 , 可能回答所有大問題 。 如果沒有其他東西 , 它是最美麗的8度模型 。 如果你沒有看到的 , 它是最美麗的8度 。
physics , science , technology	物理、科學、科學、科技、科技 。
garrett lisi on his theory of everything	伽利略在他的理論上 。
whoa , dude . check out those killer equations . sweet .	哇 , ~ ~ 那些殺人方程式 。
actually , for the next 18 minutes i'm going to do the best i can to describe the beauty of particle physics without equations .	事實上 , 接下來18分鐘我要做最好的我可以描述粒子物理學的美麗 。
it turns out there's a lot we can learn from coral .	結果發現 , 有很多我們可以從珊瑚身上學到的 。
coral is a very beautiful and unusual animal .	珊瑚是非常美麗的動物 。
each coral head consists of thousand of individual polyps .	每個珊瑚頭部都有數千個個人的頭部 。
these polyps are continually budding and branching into genetically identical neighbors .	這些都是持續虐待和鳥類的鄰居 , 讓基因移植到基因上 。
if we imagine this to be a hyperintelligent coral , we can single out an individual and ask him a reasonable question .	如果我們想像一下這個目標 , 我們就可以單獨的珊瑚 , 我們可以獨立一個個人 , 並問他一個理由的問題來問他一個理由的問題 。
we can ask how exactly he got to be in this particular location compared to his neighbors if it was just chance , or destiny , or what ?	我們可以問他他如何在這個特定的鄰居 , 如果它只是機會 , 或慾望 , 或慾望 , 或否則呢 ?
now , after admonishing us for turning the temperature up too high , he would tell us that our question was completely stupid .	現在 , 在一個怪獸之後 , 他會告訴我們 , 我們的問題很愚蠢 , 他會告訴我們 , 我們的問題完全愚蠢 。
these corals can be quite kind of mean , you see , and i have surfing scars to prove that .	這些珊瑚可能很像這樣 , 而且我有驚訝的 , 我有驚訝 。
but this polyp would continue and tell us that his neighbors were quite clearly identical copies of him .	但這可能持續 , 告訴我們他的鄰居很明顯地 , 他的鄰居是非常清楚的 。
that he was in all these other locations as well , but experiencing them as separate individuals .	他也在這些其他地方的失敗 , 但擴展了他們身為分分分分離 。
for a coral , branching into different copies is the most natural thing in the world .	對珊瑚而言 , 鳥類在世界中最自然的事情是最自然的事情 。
unlike us , a hyperintelligent coral would be uniquely prepared to understand quantum mechanics .	不像我們一樣 , 一個高度的珊瑚會很獨特地準備好去了解量量量子機械 。
the mathematics of quantum mechanics very accurately describes how our universe works .	量子機械機械非常精確地描述我們的宇宙如何運作 。
and it tells us our reality is continually branching into different possibilities , just like a coral .	它告訴我們我們的現實是完全奇怪的可能性 , 就像珊瑚一樣 。
it's a weird thing for us humans to wrap our minds around , since we only ever get to experience one possibility .	這是對我們人類的思維 , 因為我們只能經歷一個可能性 , 因為我們只能經歷一個可能性 。
this quantum weirdness was first described by erwin schrödinger and his cat .	這個量子奇怪是第一種描述者 , 他的貓咪和他的貓 。
the cat likes this version better .	像這個版本更好 。
in this setup , schrödinger is in a box with a radioactive sample that , by the laws of quantum mechanics , branches into a state in which it is radiated and a state in which it is not .	在這個組合中 , chrdinger是一個無線機機的盒子裡 , 由量子機械定律、鳥類、鳥類的法律 , 沒有 。
in the branch in which the sample radiates , it sets off a trigger that releases poison and schrödinger is dead .	在這個樣本中 , 它在沙漠中 , 它讓釋放出一個蛋白質和chrddinger是死的 。
but in the other branch of reality , he remains alive .	但在現實中 , 他仍然活著 。
these realities are experienced separately by each individual .	這些真實性都被彼此分離 。
as far as either can tell , the other one doesn't exist .	如同either可以說說 , 另一位不存在 。
this seems weird to us , because each of us only experiences an individual existence , and we don't get to see other branches .	這似乎很奇怪 , 因為每個人只經歷一個個人存在的存在 , 而且我們不會看到其他陌生人 。
it's as if each of us , like schrödinger here , are a kind of coral branching into different possibilities .	如同我們每個人一樣 , 像是chrddingerdinger , 有點像珊瑚鳥一樣 。
the mathematics of quantum mechanics tells us this is how the world works at tiny scales .	量子機械學告訴我們這是世界上最小的規模 。
it can be summed up in a single sentence: everything that can happen , does .	這可能是單一句句句話:所有可以發生的事 。
but this does not mean everything happens .	但這並不意味著一切發生 。
the rest of physics is about describing what can happen and what can't .	物理學的其他部分是關於描述什麼可能發生的事 , 以及無法做到的事 。
what physics tells us is that everything comes down to geometry and the interactions of elementary particles .	物理告訴我們的是 , 一切都會下下下降到數位粒子和互動的互動 。
and things can happen only if these interactions are perfectly balanced .	如果這些互動是完全平衡的平衡 。
now i'll go ahead and describe how we know about these particles , what they are and how this balance works .	現在我會走進一步 , 描述我們如何了解這些粒子的運作方式 , 他們是如何運作的 。
in this machine , a beam of protons and antiprotons are accelerated to near the speed of light and brought together in a collision , producing a burst of pure energy .	在這個機器中 , 有一塊蛋白質和螞蟻的速度被加速到附近的速度 , 並在一個冷靜能量中 , 促進一個冷靜的能量 。
this energy is immediately converted into a spray of subatomic particles , with detectors and computers used to figure out their properties .	這能量是將將將粒子轉化成一個小粒子的粒子 , 用偵測器和電腦用來找出他們的特性 。
this enormous machine the large hadron collider at cern in geneva has a circumference of 17 miles and , when it's operating , draws five times as much power as the city of monterey .	這個巨大的機器中 , 大型的鐵路上有17英哩 , 當它正在操作時 , 畫出五倍的力量 , 畫出五倍的力量 。
we can't predict specifically what particles will be produced in any individual collision .	我們無法預測特定的粒子會在任何個體中產生的粒子 。
quantum mechanics tells us all possibilities are realized .	量子機械告訴我們所有可能都意識到 。
but physics does tell us what particles can be produced .	但物理學會告訴我們粒子有什麼粒子 。
these particles must have just as much mass and energy as is carried in by the proton and antiproton .	這些粒子一定只是質量和能量一樣 。
any particles more massive than this energy limit aren't produced , and remain invisible to us .	任何粒子比這種能量限制並不產生 , 而我們仍然無法想像的 。
this is why this new particle accelerator is so exciting .	這就是為什麼這個新粒子的新粒子非常興奮 。
it's going to push this energy limit seven times beyond what's ever been done before , so we're going to get to see some new particles very soon .	要把這個能量推進這個能量限制了7倍 , 所以我們將會看到一些新粒子非常快 。
but before talking about what we might see , let me describe the particles we already know of .	但在談論我們所看到的 , 讓我描述我們已經知道的粒子 。
there's a whole zoo of subatomic particles .	有一系列的物質粒子 。
most of us are familiar with electrons .	我們大多數人都熟悉電子 。
a lot of people in this room make a good living pushing them around .	在這個房間裡有很多人 , 讓他們更好的生活流動 。
but the electron also has a neutral partner called the neutrino , with no electric charge and a very tiny mass .	但電子電子也有一個中央夥伴叫做 「 鄰里 」 , 沒有電荷和一個非常小小的質量 。
in contrast , the upanddown quarks have very large masses , and combine in threes to make the protons and neutrons inside atoms .	在矛盾中 , 沙丘裡有非常大的大量 , 三種可以讓蛋白質和中間的組合 。
all of these matter particles come in left and righthanded varieties , and have antiparticle partners that carry opposite charges .	所有這些物質粒子都來自左邊和右邊的各種粒子 , 帶著一種抗生素鏈 。
these familiar particles also have less familiar second and third generations , which have the same charges as the first but have much higher masses .	這些熟悉粒子粒子也較少熟悉第二代的粒子 , 相同的椅子 , 正如第一 , 但有較高的質量 。
these matter particles all interact with the various force particles .	這些物質粒子都與不同的粒子互動 。
the electromagnetic force interacts with electrically charged matter via particles called photons .	電磁力與電磁力相互作用 , 稱為 「 光子 」 的粒子 。
there is also a very weak force called , rather unimaginatively , the weak force , that interacts only with lefthanded matter .	還有一種非常震撼的力量 , 而不是想像力 , 而是左邊的弱點 , 而是左撇子左撇子 。
the strong force acts between quarks which carry a different kind of charge , called color charge , and come in three different varieties: red , green and blue .	夸克之間的強大力量 , 帶著不同的椅子 , 叫做 「 查爾 」 、綠色、綠色、藍色、藍色、藍色和藍色 。
you can blame murray gellmann for these names they're his fault .	你可以為這些名字 , 為這些名字 , 他們是他的錯的 。
finally , there's the force of gravity , which interacts with matter via its mass and spin .	最後 , 有重力的力量 , 它與視覺互動 。
the most important thing to understand here is that there's a different kind of charge associated with each of these forces .	最重要的是 , 了解到這裡有不同的挑戰 。
these four different forces interact with matter according to the corresponding charges that each particle has .	這四種不同的力量與重要性交互作用 , 每粒粒粒粒子之間的反應 。
a particle that hasn't been seen yet , but we're pretty sure exists , is the higgs particle , which gives masses to all these other particles .	粒子沒有看過 , 但我們很確定存在 , 就是暗示粒子粒子粒子粒子的粒子 。
the main purpose of the large hadron collider is to see this higgs particle , and we're almost certain it will .	大型的原則是要看到這個希格斯粒子粒子 , 我們幾乎確定它會發生 。
but the greatest mystery is what else we might see .	但最棒的謎題是其他我們所看到的 。
and i'm going to show you one beautiful possibility towards the end of this talk .	我要給各位看一個美麗的可能性 。
now , if we count up all these different particles using their various spins and charges , there are 226 .	如果我們把這些不同的粒子和椅子使用不同的粒子和椅子 , 有226 。
that's a lot of particles to keep track of .	這是很多粒子可以繼續追蹤 。
and it seems strange that nature would have so many elementary particles .	它似乎很奇怪的粒子會有很多元素 。
but if we plot them out according to their charges , some beautiful patterns emerge .	但如果我們把他們放到椅子上 , 有些美麗的模式 , 有些美麗的模式 。
the most familiar charge is electric charge .	最熟悉的椅子是電荷 。
electrons have an electric charge , a negative one , and quarks have electric charges in thirds .	電子有電荷有一個電荷 , 一個負面的負面鏈 , 三分之三 。
so when two up quarks and a down quark are combined to make a proton , it has a total electric charge of plus one .	所以 , 當兩公尺後 , 下方方方方塊就會組成一個原子電池 , 它必須用電力來製造一個鍵盤 。
these particles also have antiparticles , which have opposite charges .	這些粒子也有抗生素 , 它有相反的椅子 。
now , it turns out the electric charge is actually a combination of two other charges: hypercharge and weak charge .	結果發現 , 電鏈其實是兩種其他椅子:hypercharge和弱弱點 。
if we spread out the hypercharge and weak charge and plot the charges of particles in this twodimensional charge space , the electric charge is where these particles sit along the vertical direction .	如果我們把hypercharge和弱弱弱弱勢帶到這兩個粒子的椅子 , 電動椅子在垂直空間中 , 電荷的電荷是這些粒子坐在垂直方向上 。
the electromagnetic and weak forces interact with matter according to their hypercharge and weak charge , which make this pattern .	電磁振動器和弱弱弱勢互動 , 讓它們互動變得更重要 。
this is called the unified electroweak model , and it was put together back in 1967 .	這叫做 「 無知電模型 」 模型就在1967年 。
the reason most of us are only familiar with electric charge and not both of these is because of the higgs particle .	我們大多數人都只熟悉電鏈的原因 , 而不是兩個粒子的粒子 。
the higgs , over here on the left , has a large mass and breaks the symmetry of this electroweak pattern .	左邊 , 在左邊 , 有一個很大的和突破模式的對稱 。
it makes the weak force very weak by giving the weak particles a large mass .	它讓弱勢力變得非常弱弱勢 。
since this massive higgs sits along the horizontal direction in this diagram , the photons of electromagnetism remain massless and interact with electric charge along the vertical direction in this charge space .	從這個角度來看 , 在這個圖片中 , 電磁共振造影 , 電磁共振的光子 , 電磁共振造影機的光子 , 與電荷之間的互動 。
so the electromagnetic and weak forces are described by this pattern of particle charges in twodimensional space .	所以電磁性和弱弱勢力被描述成兩度空間的形式
we can include the strong force by spreading out its two charge directions and plotting the charges of the force particles in quarks along these directions .	我們可以藉由傳播出來 , 藉由傳播出來的力量 , 讓粒子粒子粒子在平方方方塊上 。
the charges of all known particles can be plotted in a fourdimensional charge space , and projected down to two dimensions like this so we can see them .	所有人都知道粒子可以在四度空間中被淹沒在四度空間中 , 把它們放到兩度空間 , 這樣我們就能看到它們 。
whenever particles interact , nature keeps things in a perfect balance along all four of these charge directions .	當粒子互動時 , 自然自然會持續在一個完美平衡的平衡 。
if a particle and an antiparticle collide , it creates a burst of energy and a total charge of zero in all four charge directions .	如果粒子和一個抗體的粒子 , 它會創造出一種能量 , 它創造出了一塊能量 , 每四個椅子的方向 。
at this point , anything can be created as long as it has the same energy and maintains a total charge of zero .	在這一刻 , 任何東西都能創造更長的時間 , 維持零件 。
for example , this weak force particle and its antiparticle can be created in a collision .	舉例來說 , 這個弱勢粒子可以在一個冷漠中創造出來的粒子 。
in further interactions , the charges must always balance .	在更進一步的互動中 , 椅子一定總是平衡 。
one of the weak particles could decay into an electron and an antineutrino , and these three still add to zero total charge .	其中一個粒子可以把粒子放進電子和一個螞蟻一樣 , 這三隻三隻仍然加上了零件 。
nature always keeps a perfect balance .	自然總是保持完美的平衡 。
so these patterns of charges are not just pretty .	所以這些椅子不僅是很棒的 。
they tell us what interactions are allowed to happen .	他們告訴我們互動的互動是怎樣的 。
and we can rotate this charge space in four dimensions to get a better look at the strong interaction , which has this nice hexagonal symmetry .	我們不能把這個椅子放在四度空間中 , 讓它更好看看強大的互動 , 這對稱是很棒的 。
in a strong interaction , a strong force particle , such as this one , interacts with a colored quark , such as this green one , to give a quark with a different color charge this red one .	在一個強大的互動中 , 一個強大的粒子 , 比如這個綠色的平方形 , 比如這個綠色的 , 給一個平方公尺 , 給一個紅色的粒子 。
and strong interactions are happening millions of times each second in every atom of our bodies , holding the atomic nuclei together .	強烈的互動正在發生數百萬次 , 每秒鐘都在核子核子核子核能 。
but these four charges corresponding to three forces are not the end of the story .	但這四個椅子對三個力量不是故事結束 。
we can also include two more charges corresponding to the gravitational force .	我們也能包含兩種慈善力量的反應 。
when we include these , each matter particle has two different spin charges , spinup and spindown .	當我們包含這些時 , 每個粒子都有兩種不同的脊髓 , 脊髓和脊髓 。
so they all split , and give a nice pattern in sixdimensional charge space .	所以他們都在拼字空間中 , 給一個很好的模式 。
we can rotate this pattern in six dimensions , and see that it's quite pretty .	我們不能把這個模式放在六度空間中 , 看看這是很棒的 。
right now , this pattern matches our best current knowledge of how nature is built at the tiny scales of these elementary particles .	現在 , 這個模式將我們最好的知識 , 大自然的知識是如何在小小小的粒子 。
this is what we know for certain .	這就是我們所知的 。
some of these particles are at the very limit of what we've been able to reach with experiments .	有些粒子在我們所擁有的一些粒子 。
from this pattern , we already know the particle physics of these tiny scales . the way the universe works with these tiny scales is very beautiful .	從這個模式中 , 我們已經知道粒子物理尺寸的粒子 。
but now i'm going to discuss some new and old ideas about things we don't know yet .	但我現在要討論一些新的想法 , 關於我們不知道的東西 。
we want to expand this pattern using mathematics alone , and see if we can get our hands on the whole enchilada .	我們想要擴展這個模式 , 用數學來解釋這個模式 , 如果我們能把手放在整個en晶片上 。
we want to find all the particles and forces that make a complete picture of our universe .	我們想要找到所有的粒子和力量 , 讓宇宙完全相似的圖像 。
and we want to use this picture to predict new particles that we'll see when experiments reach higher energies .	我們想要用這張照片來預測新的粒子 。
so there's an old idea in particle physics that this known pattern of charges , which is not very symmetric , could emerge from a more perfect pattern that gets broken similar to how the higgs particle breaks the electroweak pattern to give electromagnetism .	所以 , 粒子物理學中有一個古老的想法 , 這不是非常合理的形式 , 而是可以從一個更完美的模式 , 可以從一個更完美的模式 , 可以從更完美的形式 , 讓昆蟲分解出電磁振圖案 。
in order to do this , we need to introduce new forces with new charge directions .	為了做到這一點 , 我們需要引導新的領導力 。
when we introduce a new direction , we get to guess what charges the particles have along this direction , and then we can rotate it in with the others .	當我們介紹一個新的方向時 , 我們必須猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜猜
if we guess wisely , we can construct the standard charges in six charge dimensions as a broken symmetry of this more perfect pattern in seven charge dimensions .	如果我們猜想一下 , 我們就能建構標準標準的標準標準標準標準的標準 。
this particular choice corresponds to a grand unified theory introduced by pati and salam in 1973 .	這種特定的企業家 , 由patiti和1973年的理論 。
when we look at this new unified pattern , we can see a couple of gaps where particles seem to be missing .	當我們觀察這個新統計模式時 , 我們可以看到粒子的粒子似乎被誤解 。
this is the way theories of unification work .	這是不可思議的工作的方式 。
a physicist looks for larger , more symmetric patterns that include the established pattern as a subset .	物理學家尋找更大的稱性模式 , 包括 「 物質 」 的模式 , 包括 「 潛水 」 的模式 」 。
the larger pattern allows us to predict the existence of particles that have never been seen .	最大的模式讓我們預測粒子存在於粒子的存在 。
this unification model predicts the existence of these two new force particles , which should act a lot like the weak force , only weaker .	這兩個新的粒子模型預測預測存在於兩種新粒子的存在 , 它應該會像弱弱勢一樣 。
now we can rotate this set of charges in seven dimensions and consider an odd fact about the matter particles: the second and third generations of matter have exactly the same charges in sixdimensional charge space as the first generation .	現在我們不能把這個椅子放在七度空間中 , 考慮粒子的事實:第二、第三代、第三代、第三代、第三代的重要性 。
these particles are not uniquely identified by their six charges .	這些粒子不是獨特地辨識到六個椅子 。
they sit on top of one another in the standard charge space .	他們坐在標準空間的頂端 。
however , if we work in eightdimensional charge space , then we can assign unique new charges to each particle .	然而 , 如果我們在八度空間中工作 , 那麼我們可以忽略獨特的新椅子 , 讓每個粒子獨特的新椅子 。
then we can spin these in eight dimensions , and see what the whole pattern looks like .	接著 , 我們可以在八度內這些模式中 , 看看整個模式是什麼樣子 。
here we can see the second and third generations of matter now related to the first generation by a symmetry called " triality . "	我們可以看到第二代和第三代的重要世代 , 稱之為 「 虛擬 」 。
this particular pattern of charges in eight dimensions is actually part of the most beautiful geometric structure in mathematics .	這個特定模式是8度最美麗的圖案其實是數學最美麗的結構 。
it's a pattern of the largest exceptional lie group , e8 .	這是一群最大的執行模式 , 8.
this lie group is a smooth , curved shape with 248 dimensions .	這個謊言團是一個抽菸、治癒248度形狀 。
each point in this pattern corresponds to a symmetry of this very complex and beautiful shape .	在這個模式中 , 每個角落都有這種複雜且美麗的形狀 。
one small part of this e8 shape can be used to describe the curved spacetime of einstein's general relativity , explaining gravity .	其中一小部分的形狀可以用來描述蛋白質的曲線 , 解釋了重力 。
together with quantum mechanics , the geometry of this shape could describe everything about how the universe works at the tiniest scales .	用量子力學 , 這種形狀可以描述宇宙如何運作宇宙運作的一切 。
the pattern of this shape living in eightdimensional charge space is exquisitely beautiful , and it summarizes thousands of possible interactions between these elementary particles , each of which is just a facet of this complicated shape .	這個形狀在八度空間中形成的形狀很漂亮 , 而且它突然形成數千種可能性粒子之間的互動 , 每個元素之間的互動 。
as we spin it , we can see many of the other intricate patterns contained in this one .	當我們把它放進去 , 我們可以看到許多其他特徵的模式 。
and with a particular rotation , we can look down through this pattern in eight dimensions along a symmetry axis and see all the particles at once .	有一種特殊的動作 , 我們可以在八度內觀察這個模式中 , 看到所有粒子的粒子 , 看到所有粒子的粒子 。
it's a very beautiful object , and as with any unification , we can see some holes where new particles are required by this pattern .	這是個非常美麗的物體 , 我們可以看到一些洞穴 , 新粒子需要的洞見 。
there are 20 gaps where new particles should be , two of which have been filled by the patisalam particles .	有20個差距應該是新粒子 , 新粒子應該被固定的粒子 。
from their location in this pattern , we know that these new particles should be scalar fields like the higgs particle , but have color charge and interact with the strong force .	在這個模式中 , 我們知道這些新粒子應該被嚇壞的粒子 , 像是希格粒子粒子粒子 , 但有顏色的力量 。
filling in these new particles completes this pattern , giving us the full e8 .	在這些新粒子裡 , 把我們整合起來 , 讓我們整8 。
this e8 pattern has very deep mathematical roots .	這個選項非常深的數學根源 。
it's considered by many to be the most beautiful structure in mathematics .	它被很多人認為是數學上最美麗的結構 。
it's a fantastic prospect that this object of great mathematical beauty could describe the truth of particle interactions at the smallest scales imaginable .	這是個很棒的數學證明 , 這個物體可以描述粒子的真相可以描述粒子互動的真相 。
and this idea that nature is described by mathematics is not at all new .	這點子是由數學描述的 , 不是全新的 。
in 1623 , galileo wrote this: " nature's grand book , which stands continually open to our gaze , is written in the language of mathematics .	在1623年 , 伽利略寫了這個: 「 大自然的書 」 的本書 , 一直在開放數學語言中寫的語言 。
its characters are triangles , circles and other geometrical figures , without which it is humanly impossible to understand a single word of it ; without these , one is wandering around in a dark labyrinth . "	它的角色是三角形 , 圓圈和其他幾何形狀 , 沒有人是不可能理解它的單一詞 ; 沒有這些 , 沒有人在黑暗實驗室裡 。 」
i believe this to be true , and i've tried to follow galileo's guidance in describing the mathematics of particle physics using only triangles , circles and other geometrical figures .	我相信這是真的 , 我試著遵循grio的指導 , 在描述數學上 , 只用三角形來描述數學數字 , 圓圈和其他幾何學位 。
of course , when other physicists and i actually work on this stuff , the mathematics can resemble a dark labyrinth .	當然 , 當我其他物理學家 , 我真的在這個東西上工作時 , 數學可以重新組成黑暗實驗室 。
but it's reassuring that at the heart of this mathematics is pure , beautiful geometry .	但 , 在數學的心臟中 , 令人驚訝的是 , 美麗的幾何神奇 。
joined with quantum mechanics , this mathematics describes our universe as a growing e8 coral , with particles interacting at every location in all possible ways according to a beautiful pattern .	加入量量子機械 , 這個數學描述我們的宇宙形式 , 和粒子之間的互動 , 粒子互相互動 。
and as more of the pattern comes into view using new machines like the large hadron collider , we may be able to see whether nature uses this e8 pattern or a different one .	隨著更多的模式進入使用新機器 , 比如大型的鐵路 , 我們可能可以看到大自然使用這個時代 , 或不同的人 。
this process of discovery is a wonderful adventure to be involved in .	這種發現發現是一種很棒的冒險 。
if the lhc finds particles that fit this e8 pattern , that will be very , very cool .	如果lhc找到粒子的粒子 , 那就會非常酷 。
if the lhc finds new particles , but they don't fit this pattern well , that will be very interesting , but bad for this e8 theory .	如果lhc找到新的粒子 , 但它們並不符合這個模式 , 那將會非常有趣 , 但對這個選項很有趣 。
and , of course , bad for me personally .	當然 , 對我來說 , 對於我個人來說很糟糕 。
now how bad would that be ?	那會是什麼糟糕的 ?
well , pretty bad .	嗯 , 很糟 。
but predicting how nature works is a very risky game .	但預測自然運作是非常危險的遊戲 。
this theory and others like it are long shots .	這理論和其他類似的景象 。
one does a lot of hard work knowing that most of these ideas probably won't end up being true about nature .	其中一個有許多困難的研究知道 , 大部分的想法可能不會終止是自然的 。
that's what doing theoretical physics is like: there are a lot of wipeouts .	這就是物理物理物理學的樣子 。
in this regard , new physics theories are a lot like startup companies .	在這個區域中 , 新物理學有很多類似的公司 。
as with any large investment , it can be emotionally difficult to abandon a line of research when it isn't working out .	身為任何大投資者 , 它能情緒上很難吸收 。
but in science , if something isn't working , you have to toss it out and try something else .	但在科學上 , 如果某件事沒有工作 , 你必須去嘗試其他東西 。
now , the only way to maintain sanity and achieve happiness in the midst of this uncertainty is to keep balance and perspective in life .	現在 , 為了維持聖地和成就的唯一方法就是保持平衡和尊重生活的平衡 。
i've tried the best i can to live a balanced life .	我嘗試過最好的人生 。
i try to balance my life equally between physics , love and surfing my own three charge directions .	我試著平衡我的人生平衡之間的平衡 , 愛和傷害我的三條規則 。
this way , even if the physics i work on comes to nothing , i still know i've lived a good life .	這種方式 , 即使我在來沒有什麼事 , 我仍然知道我生活過好的生活 。
and i try to live in beautiful places .	我試著住在美麗的地方 。

now it's one of the greatest mysteries in the universe to my parents how i managed to survive all that time without engaging in anything resembling fulltime employment .	這是宇宙中最偉大的謎之一 , 我父母要如何存活下來 , 不用在任何東西中 , 都沒有參與任何共享的員工之一 。

but what about how they behaved ? that's what he wanted to know .	但他們到底怎麼樣呢 ? 那是他想要知道的 。
and of course , behavior doesn't fossilize .	當然 , 行為並不是化石 。
he argued and it's now a fairly common theory that if we found behavior patterns similar or the same in our closest living relatives , the great apes , and humans today , then maybe those behaviors were present in the apelike , humanlike ancestor some seven million years ago .	他現在認為 , 如果我們發現行為模式很常見的理論理論 , 如果我們發現行為模式相似或同於我們最近的活生生生生生生存 , 那麼這些行為是人類的 , 也許這些行為是人類的 。
and therefore , perhaps we had brought those characteristics with us from that ancient , ancient past .	因此 , 也許我們帶給這些特徵、古老、古老的過去 。
well , if you look in textbooks today that deal with human evolution , you very often find people speculating about how early humans may have behaved , based on the behavior of chimpanzees .	嗯 , 如果你看看今天的書籍 , 你通常會發現人類演化的行為 , 你通常會發現人們在黑猩猩猩的行為行為 , 根據黑猩猩的行為行為行為行為行為行為行為的行為 。
they are more like us than any other living creature , and we've heard about that during this ted conference .	他們比其他生物其他生物生物一樣 , 我們聽過這個ted會議時 , 我們聽過這個ted會議 。
so it remains for me to comment on the ways in which chimpanzees are so like us , in certain aspects of their behavior .	所以 , 對我來說 , 黑猩猩來說 , 黑猩的確存在 , 就像我們一樣 , 在某些行為上 。
every chimpanzee has his or her own personality .	每隻黑猩猩有自己的個人性 。
of course , i gave them names . they can live to be 60 years or more , although we think most of them probably don't make it to 60 in the wild .	當然 , 我給他們名字
mr . wurzel . the female has her first baby when she's 11 or 12 .	mr.wurzel , 雌性是她11或12歲 。
thereafter , she has one baby only every five or six years , a long period of childhood dependency when the child is nursing , sleeping with the mother at night , and riding on her back .	在那裡 , 她有一隻嬰兒只有每五到六歲的童年 , 一個長期的期期期間 , 睡在她背後 , 和母親一起哭泣 。
and we believe that this long period of childhood is important for chimpanzees , just as it is for us , in relation to learning .	我們相信這長期期期的童年很重要 , 就像黑猩猩一樣重要 。
as the brain becomes ever more complex during evolution in different forms of animals , so we find that learning plays an ever more important role in an individual's life history .	當大腦變得更複雜 , 在演化過程中 , 我們發現學習玩耍的角色 , 所以我們發現學習扮演了更重要的角色 。
and young chimpanzees spend a lot of time watching what their elders do .	年輕黑猩花了很多時間看他們的老闆 。
we know now that they're capable of imitating behaviors that they see .	我們現在知道他們有能力的行為 。
and we believe that it's in this way that the different toolusing behaviors that have now been seen in all the different chimpanzee populations studied in africa how these are passed from one generation to the next , through observation , imitation and practice , so that we can describe these toolusing behaviors as primitive culture .	我們相信這是不同的工具 , 在非洲各地不同的黑猩研究行為 , 現在我們可以描述非洲人如何從一個世代到下一個世代 , 透過觀察和練習 , 透過觀察和練習 , 所以我們可以描述這些工具 , 我們可以描述這些工具 。
chimpanzees don't have a spoken language . we've talked about that .	黑猩猩不會有脊椎語言 。 我們已經談過這一點 。
they do have a very rich repertoire of postures and gestures , many of which are similar , or even identical , to ours and formed in the same context . greeting chimpanzees embracing .	他們有非常豐富的繁殖 , 很多類似的 , 很多類似的 , 甚至是相似的 , 甚至是同的 , 和我們的同性戀 。
they also kiss , hold hands , pat one another on the back .	他們也技巧 , 手、手、手、手、握手 ,
and they swagger and they throw rocks .	他們把火箭轉換成岩石 。
in chimpanzee society , we find many , many examples of compassion , precursors to love and true altruism .	在黑猩社會中 , 我們發現很多很多同情心、預防、預防、預防、真正的替代 。
unfortunately , they , like us , have a dark side to their nature .	不幸的是 , 他們就像我們一樣 , 有黑暗的邊緣 。
they're capable of extreme brutality , even a kind of primitive war .	他們有能力極度的戰爭 , 甚至有點荒謬 。
and these really aggressive behaviors , for the most part , are directed against individuals of the neighboring social group .	這些真的很有意見的行為 , 最重要的部分是對鄰居的社會團體 。
they are very territorially aggressive .	他們非常驚訝 。
chimpanzees , i believe , more than any other living creature , have helped us to understand that , after all , there is no sharp line between humans and the rest of the animal kingdom .	黑猩猩 , 我相信 , 比其他生物其他生物 , 幫助我們了解 , 畢竟 , 沒有鯊魚和動物界之間的連結 。
it's a very blurry line , and it's getting more blurry all the time as we make even more observations .	這是個非常盲目的線索 , 每次我們做更多的盲目 。
the study that i began in 1960 is still continuing to this day .	我在1960年代開始持續持續持續持續持續 。
and these chimpanzees , living their complex social lives in the wild , have helped more than anything else to make us realize we are part of , and not separated from , the amazing animals with whom we share the planet .	這些黑猩猩 , 牠們的複雜社會生活在野生動物身上 , 幫助我們了解到 , 我們是共同的一部分 , 而不是從我們共享的動物 。
so it's pretty sad to find that chimpanzees , like so many other creatures around the world , are losing their habitats .	所以 , 很難找到黑猩 , 就像世界上其他生物一樣 , 像許多其他生物一樣 , 失去他們的棲息 。
this is just one photograph from the air , and it shows you the forested highlands of gombe .	這只是從空氣中拍攝的照片 , 它給你看最高的目標之一 。
and it was when i flew over the whole area , about 16 years ago , and realized that outside the park , this forest , which in 1960 had stretched almost unbroken along the eastern shore of lake tanganyika , which is where the tiny , 30squaremile gombe national park lies , that a question came to my mind .	當我飛過整個區域時 , 大約16年前 , 我發現在公園裡 , 這森林外 , 在1960年間 , 這森林裡 , 發現 , 在東京的海岸岸岸岸邊 , 三十公里的海岸線 , 那是我腦海中最小的問題 。
" how can we even try to save these famous chimpanzees , when the people living around the national park are struggling to survive ? "	「 我們怎麼能拯救這些有名黑猩猩 」 時 , 當我們住在國家公園裡的人會掙扎 ? "
more people are living there than the land could possibly support .	更多人居住在那裏 , 可能是支持的 。
the numbers increased by refugees pouring in from burundi and over the lake from congo .	數量的難民會增加燃燒的數字增加 。
and very poor people they couldn't afford to buy food from elsewhere .	非常貧窮的人無法買食物從其他地方買不到食物 。
this led to a program , which we call tacare .	這導致一個計畫 , 我們稱之為 「 tacare 」 。
it's a very holistic way of improving the lives of the people living in the villages around the park .	這是一個非常榮幸的方式來改善公園的生活方式 。
it started small with 12 villages . it's now in 24 .	它從24歲到村莊 , 現在在24歲 。
there isn't time to go into it , but it's including things like tree nurseries , methods of farming most suitable to this now very degraded , almost desertlike land up in these mountains .	沒有時間去進入它 , 但它包括農業 , 包括農業、農業、農業、農業、近年級的農業 。
ways of controlling , preventing soil erosion .	控制的控制方式 , 防止土壤 。
ways of reclaiming overused farmland , so that within two years they can again be productive .	回收農場的農地 , 所以在兩年內 , 再次他們可能再次有生產力 。
working to help the villagers obtain fresh water from wells .	為了協助村民觀察者觀察者的水源 。
perhaps build some schoolrooms .	也許建造一些學校室 。
most important of all , i believe , is working with small groups of women , providing them with opportunities for microcredit loans .	最重要的是 , 我相信 , 就是和女性合作的小群體 , 提供他們機會 , 提供微信息貸貸貸款 。
and we've got , as is the case around the world , about 95 percent of all loans returned .	我們得知 , 身為世界各地的案例 , 大約95%的貸款 。
empowering women , working with education , providing scholarships for girls so they can finish secondary school , in the clear understanding that , all around the world , as women's education improves , family size drops .	賦予女性、教育、教育、教育、教育、教育、她們能完成第二個學校 , 明顯地了解 , 所有世界各地的學校 , 都是女性的教育、家庭飲食 。
we provide information about family planning and about hiv/aids .	我們提供關於家庭計劃和愛滋病的資訊 。
and as a result of this program , something's happening for conservation .	作為這個計畫的結果 , 有些事情正在發生 。
what's happening for conservation is that the farmers living in these 24 villages , instead of looking on us as a bunch of white people coming to study a whole bunch of monkeys and by the way , many of the staff are now tanzanian but when we began the tacare program , it was a tanzanian team going into the villages .	保育計畫是 , 農夫住在這24個村莊 , 而不是在看我們身邊的白人人人 , 而是當我們開始研究一群白人人人來研究一群猴子 , 但當我們開始坦尚尼亞的團隊 。
it was a tanzanian team talking to the villagers , asking what they were interested in .	這是一個坦尚尼亞的團隊 , 問他們他們他們對哪些興趣 。
were they interested in conservation ? absolutely not .	他們很感興趣嗎 ? 絕對不是 。
they were interested in health ; they were interested in education .	他們對健康有興趣 , 他們對教育有興趣 。
and as time went on , and as their situation began to improve , they began to understand ever more about the need for conservation .	隨著時間進步 , 當他們的情況開始改善 , 他們開始了解保育 , 他們開始了解保育需求的需求 。
they began to understand that as the upper levels of the hills were denuded of trees , so you've got this terrible soil erosion and mudslides .	他們開始了解到 , 山頂層的層層層 , 所以你有這種可怕的土壤和mudlidelideslideslideslideslides 。
today , we are developing what we call the greater gombe ecosystem .	今天 , 我們正在發展出我們稱之為 「 更好的目標 」 。
this is an area way outside the national park , stretching out into all these very degraded lands .	這是國家公園外的公園 , 站在全國公園裡 。
and as these villages have a better standard of life , they are actually agreeing to put between 10 percent and 20 percent of their land in the highlands aside , so that once again , as the trees grow back , the chimpanzees will have leafy corridors through which they can travel to interact as they must for genetic viability with other remnant groups outside the national park .	身為這些村莊有更好的標準 , 他們真的認同了10%到20%的土地上 , 所以這棵樹會再次 , 當樹林成長後 , 黑猩猩會在高島上互動時 , 黑猩猩猩猩會透過牠們的基因能力來互動 。
so tacare is a success .	所以tacare是一個成功的成功 。
we're replicating it in other parts of africa , around other wilderness areas which are faced with extreme population pressure .	我們在非洲其他地區的其他部分 , 其他見證都是極端的人口壓力 。
the problems in africa , however , as we've been discussing for the whole of these first couple of days of ted , are major problems .	然而 , 在非洲 , 我們一直在討論這些第一幾天的ted , 是主要問題 。
there is a great deal of poverty .	貧窮的貧窮 。
and when you get large numbers of people living in land that is not that fertile , particularly when you cut down trees , and you leave the soil open to the wind for erosion , as desperate populations cut down more and more trees , so that they can try and grow food for themselves and their families , what's going to happen ? something's got to give .	當你在土地上得到大量的人們 , 特別是當你砍伐樹的時候 , 特別是當你砍伐樹木時 , 你就離開了土壤 , 使人口砍伐更多樹木 , 所以他們可以嘗試和食物 , 然後他們家人 , 該怎麼做 ?
and the other problems in not only africa , but the rest of the developing world and , indeed , everywhere what are we doing to our planet ?	而不是非洲其他問題 , 而是開發中國家的其他問題 , 而是在於開發中國家 , 我們在做什麼 ?
you know , the famous scientist , e . o . wilson said that if every person on this planet attains the standard of living of the average european or american , we need three new planets .	你知道嗎 , 歐元科學家 , 歐巴森說 , 如果每個人在這個星球的標準 , 我們需要三個新的星球的標準 。
today , they are saying four . but we don't have them . we've got one .	今天 , 他們說四歲 , 但我們沒有他們 。
and what's happened ? i mean , the question here is , here we are , arguably the most intelligent being that's ever walked planet earth , with this extraordinary brain , capable of the kind of technology that is so well illustrated by these ted conferences , and yet we're destroying the only home we have .	發生了什麼事 ? 我的意思是 , 問題是 , 我們在哪裡走過地球上最聰明的大腦 , 和這個極端的大腦 , 可以用這種技術來吸引地球 , 但是我們正在摧毀地球上唯一的家園 , 但我們正在摧毀我們唯一的家 。
the indigenous people around the world , before they made a major decision , used to sit around and ask themselves , " how does this decision affect our people seven generations ahead ? "	在世界各地的人身上 , 在他們做了一個主要決策之前 , 請問自己: 「 這決定如何影響我們的七代代人 ? 」
today , major decisions and i'm not particularly talking about africa here , but the developed world major decisions involving millions of dollars , and millions of people , are often based on , " how will this affect the next shareholders' meeting ? "	今天 , 主要決策 , 我不是特別談論非洲 , 而是開發了數百萬美金 , 而是開發了數百萬美元 , 通常是基於: 「 接下來會如何影響下下下一個共享者 ? 」
and these decisions affect africa .	這些決策影響非洲 。
as i began traveling around africa talking about the problems faced by chimpanzees and their vanishing forests , i realized more and more how so many of africa's problems could be laid at the door of previous colonial exploitation .	當我開始在非洲各地的談話時 , 我了解到更多的非洲和他們的優勢 , 我意識到更多的非洲問題 , 更多的非洲問題可能是多麼嚴重的 。
so i began traveling outside africa , talking in europe , talking in the united states , going to asia .	所以我開始到非洲 , 和歐洲談話 , 談到亞洲 , 談到亞洲 。
and everywhere there were these terrible problems .	任何地方都有這些可怕的問題 。
and you know the kind i'm talking about . i'm talking about pollution .	你知道我正在談論污染污染污染污染 。
the air that we breathe that often poisons us .	我們呼吸 , 通常我們呼吸的空氣 。
the earth is poisoning our foods .	地球正在污染我們的食物 。
the water water is perhaps one of the most crucial issues that we're going to face in this century and everywhere water is being polluted by agricultural , industrial and household chemicals that still are being sprayed around the world , seemingly with the inability to profit from past experience .	水是 , 我們要面對這個世紀最關鍵的問題之一就是農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業、農業
the mangroves are being cut down ; the effects of things like the tsunami get worse .	曼格魯斯已經被砍掉 , 像是海嘯更糟 。
we've talked about the soil erosion .	我們談到土壤的土壤 。
we have the reckless burning of fossil fuels along with other greenhouse gasses , so called , leading to climate change .	我們有無憂的石油燃料燃料燃料燃料 , 稱為氣候變遷 。
finally , all around the world , people have begun to believe that there is something going on very wrong with our climate .	最後 , 世界各地 , 人們都對我們的氣候非常錯誤 。
all around the world climates are mixed up .	世界各地氣候被混合起來 。
and it's the poor people who are affected worse .	這是那些影響最糟糕的人 。
it's africa that already is affected .	非洲已經影響了 。
in many parts of subsaharan africa , the droughts are so much worse .	在撒哈拉非洲 , 許多地方帶來了非常糟糕 。
and when the rain does come , it so often leads to flooding and added distress , and the cycle of poverty and hunger and disease .	當雨林發生時 , 通常會導致洪水 , 會導致貧窮和飢餓、飢餓、飢餓和疾病的循環 。
and the numbers of people living in an area that the land cannot support , who are too poor to buy food , who can't move away because the whole land is degraded .	而住在一個島嶼裡的人數數數數量的人數數數數量太貧窮了 , 因為整個土地被摧毀 。
and so you get desertification creeping , creeping , creeping as the last of the trees are cut down .	所以 , 你得到更嚴重的危機 , 回應樹木的最後一棵樹被砍掉 。
and this kind of thing is not just in africa . it's all over the world .	這類事情不只是在非洲各地 。
so it wasn't surprising to me that as i was traveling around the world i met so many young people who seemed to have lost hope .	所以這不是讓我驚訝的是 , 當我在世界各地旅行時 , 我遇到許多年輕人似乎失去希望 。
we seem to have lost wisdom , the wisdom of the indigenous people .	我們似乎失去智慧、智慧、智慧的智慧 。
i asked a question . " why ? "	我問一個問題: 「 為什麼 ? 」
well , do you think there could be some kind of disconnect between this extraordinarily clever brain , the kind of brain that the ted technologies exemplify , and the human heart ? talking about it in the nonscientific term , in terms of love and compassion . is there some disconnect ?	嗯 , 你認為有某種程度的分析 , 在ted的大腦中 , 有某種程度上 , ted科技的大腦 , 人類的心智和同情心 , 談到愛和同情心 , 談到愛和同情心 。
and these young people , when i talk to them , basically they were either depressed or apathetic , or bitter and angry . and they said more or less the same thing , " we feel this way because we feel you've compromised our future and there's nothing we can do about it . "	這些年輕人 , 當我跟他們談話時 , 他們基本上是憂鬱或憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒、憤怒 。 」
we have compromised their future .	我們有複雜的未來 。
i've got three little grandchildren , and every time i look at them and i think how we've harmed this beautiful planet since i was their age , i feel this desperation .	我有三個小的孫子 , 每次我看著他們 , 我想我們如何傷害這個美麗的星球 , 因為我是他們的年齡 , 我覺得這是他們的需求 。
and that led to this program we call roots and shoots , which began right here in tanzania and has now spread to 97 countries around the world .	這個計畫讓我們稱之為根廷和拍攝的計畫 , 這開始在坦尚尼亞和全世界傳播到97個國家 。
it's symbolic . roots make a firm foundation .	它是對象性的 。 根根根根除一個奇怪的基礎 。
shoots seem tiny ; to reach the sun they can break through a brick wall .	攝影似乎很小 ; 到太陽能板牆壁裡打破一個磚牆 。
see the brick wall as all these problems we've inflicted on the planet , environmental and social . it's a message of hope .	看看我們在地球上所有問題的磚牆上 , 環境和社會 。 這是一種希望的訊息 。
hundreds and thousands of young people around the world can break through and can make this a better world for all living things .	全世界有數百名年輕人都可以破壞這個世界 , 可以讓這更好的世界變得更好的世界 。
the most important message of roots and shoots: every single one of us makes a difference , every single day .	最重要的訊息和根根根源:每一天 , 我們都會做出差異 , 每天都有差異 。
we have a choice . every one of us in this room , we have a choice as to what kind of difference we want to make .	我們有選擇 。 我們每個人都有選擇 。
the very poor have no choice . it's up to us to change things so that the poor have choice as well .	窮人沒有選擇
the roots and shoots groups all choose three projects .	根部和槍擊團團團體都選了三項項計畫 。
it depends on how old they are , and which country , whether they're in a city or rural , as to what kinds of projects .	它依賴他們多久 , 而國家 , 不論他們在城市或鄉村 , 不論他們是怎麼樣的 。
but basically , we have programs now from preschool right through university , with more and more adults starting their own roots and shoots groups .	但基本上 , 我們現在從預防大學畢業 , 從準備開始 , 越來越多的成年人開始 , 拍攝他們的根部和槍擊團團團體 。
and every group chooses , between them , three different kinds of project to make this a better world , recognizing that all these different problems are interconnected and impinge on each other .	每組組選項之間 , 三種不同的計畫 , 讓這個更好的世界變得更好的世界 , 了解彼此之間的聯繫 。
so one of their projects will be to help their own human community .	所以 , 他們的專案之一會協助自己自己自己的社區 。

artist dianna cohen shares some tough truths about plastic pollution in the ocean and in our lives and some thoughts on how to free ourselves from the plastic gyre .	藝術家納納納納森分享一些關於塑膠污染污染的真相 , 在我們的生活中 , 有些想在塑膠玻璃上 。
consumerism , global issues , green , mission blue , oceans , plastic	消費者主義、全球議題、綠色、海洋、海洋、塑膠、塑膠、塑膠、塑膠 。
dianna cohen: tough truths about plastic pollution	狄安娜•安娜:很難真理的真相 。
i'm a visual artist , and i'm also one of the cofounders of the plastic pollution coalition .	我是個視覺藝術家 , 我也是其中之一 。
i've been working with plastic bags , which i cut up and sew back together as my primary material for my artwork for the last 20 years .	我和塑膠袋一起合作 , 我把塑膠袋放在過去二十年裡 , 把我當作藝術作品放在我的藝術作品中 。
i turn them into two and threedimensional pieces and sculptures and installations .	我把它們轉為兩、三維空間和雕塑和雕塑和雕塑 。
upon working with the plastic , after about the first eight years , some of my work started to fissure and break down into smaller little bits of plastic .	一開始塑膠塑膠 , 大約八年後 , 有些我的工作開始吸收塑膠 。
and i thought , " great .	我心想: 「 好 。 」
it's ephemeral just like us . "	它就像我們一樣 。 」
upon educating myself a little further about plastics , i actually realized this was a bad thing .	在教育中 , 我意識到 , 關於塑膠 , 我其實意識到這是一件壞事 。
it's a bad thing that plastic breaks down into smaller little bits , because it's always still plastic .	塑膠突破成更小的東西 , 因為它總是總是塑膠 。
and what we're finding is that a lot of it is in the marine environment .	我們發現的是海洋環境中有很多 。
i then , in the last few years , learned about the pacific garbage patch and the gyre .	然後 , 在過去幾年裡 , 學到關於太平洋的禮物 。
and my initial reaction and i think this is a lot of people's first reaction to learning about it is , " oh my god !	而我認為這是許多人的反應 , 我認為這是很多人第一個反應 , 「 噢 ! 我的天啊 !
we've got to go out there and clean this thing up . "	我們必須走出去 , 清潔這個東西 。 」
so i actually developed a proposal to go out with a cargo ship and two decommissioned fishing trawlers , a crane , a chipping machine and a coldmolding machine .	所以 , 我實際上開發了一個建議 , 兩度辯論的船隻 , 一隻螃蟹 , 一隻螃蟹 , 一隻螃蟹 , 一隻螃蟹機器和蟻群 。
and my intention was to go out to the gyre , raise awareness about this issue and begin to pick up the plastic , chip it into little bits and cold mold it into bricks that could potentially be used as building materials in underdeveloped communities .	而我的意見是要走出gyreyreis的意識 , 開始把這個議題放到塑膠、雞蛋 , 把它當作材料當作建築物中的材料 , 可能會被用來用來用來用來建造材料的材料 。
i began talking with people who actually had been out to the gyre and were studying the plastic problem in the marine environment and upon doing so , i realized actually that cleaning it up would be a very small drop in the bucket relative to how much is being generated every day around the world , and that actually i needed to back up and look at the bigger picture .	我開始跟大家聊天的人們談話 , 研究海洋環境中的塑膠問題 , 在海洋環境中 , 我發現它乾淨的塑膠問題 , 我真的意識到 , 將它帶回世界各地的每一天 , 我真的需要回到世界各地的照片 。
and the bigger picture is: we need to find a way to turn off the faucet .	更大的照片是:我們需要找到方法的方法 。
we need to cut the spigot of singleuse and disposable plastics , which are entering the marine environment every day on a global scale .	我們需要把單位切割和可避免塑膠的塑膠 , 每天都進入全球規模的海洋環境 。
so in looking at that , i also realized that i was really angry .	看看這一點 , 我也意識到我真的很憤怒 。
i wasn't just concerned about plastic that you're trying to imagine out in the middle of the pacific ocean of which i have learned there are now 11 gyres , potentially , of plastic in five major oceans in the world .	我不只是擔心塑膠海洋中間的塑膠海洋中間 , 我學到的塑膠海洋中間有11個玻璃 , 可能是現在世界上有11度的塑膠 。
it's not just that gyre of plastic that i'm concerned about it's the gyre of plastic in the supermarket .	不只是塑膠我所擔心的塑膠 , 而是在超市塑膠中的塑膠 。
i'd go to the supermarket and all of my food is packaged in plastic .	我要去超市超市和所有食物都包裝了 。
all of my beverages are packaged in plastic , even at the health food market .	我所有人都在塑膠市場上包裝 , 即使在健康市場市場上 。
i'm also concerned about the plastic in the refrigerator , and i'm concerned about the plastic and the toxins that leach from plastic into us and into our bodies .	我也關心了塑膠和墨西哥灣的塑膠和墨西哥灣的塑膠和毒素有關 。
so i came together with a group of other people who were all looking at this issue , and we created the plastic pollution coalition .	所以我和一群人一起研究這個議題 , 我們創造了塑膠污染煤炭 。
we have many initiatives that we're working on , but some of them are very basic .	我們有許多正面的感知 , 但有些是非常基本的 。
one is: if 80 to 90 percent of what we're finding in the ocean of the marine debris that we're finding in the ocean is plastic , then why don't we call it what it is .	第一:如果80%到海洋中發現我們在海洋中發現我們在海洋中發現的海洋是塑膠 , 那麼為什麼我們不稱它為它為甚麼 。
recycling everybody kind of ends their books about being sustainable and greening with the idea of recycling .	回收每個人的書籍 , 關於保持穩定和綠色的概念 。
you put something in a bin and you don't have to think about it again .	你把東西放進蛋白質放進蛋白質放在一起 。
what is the reality of that ?	那到底是什麼 ?
in the united states , less than seven percent of our plastics are recycled .	在美國 , 超過70%的塑膠是回收的 。
and if you really look into it , particularly when it comes to plastic bottles , most of it is only downcycled , or incinerated , or shipped to china .	如果你仔細觀察它 , 特別是當它來塑膠瓶 , 大部分是唯一的循環 , 或是中國 。
it is downcycled and turned into lesser things , while a glass bottle can be a glass bottle again or can be used again a plastic bottle can never be a plastic bottle again .	它被降低 , 轉化成較少的東西 , 雖然玻璃瓶可以再再一次地用塑膠瓶瓶 , 再再再一次一次塑膠瓶 , 再再再一次塑膠瓶 。
so this is a big issue for us .	這就是我們對我們來說 。
another thing that we're looking at and asking people to think about is we've added a fourth r onto the front of the " reduce , reuse , recycle , " three r's , and that is refuse .	另一件事 , 我們正在看著人們去思考的是我們在 「 紅色 」 的第四個r , 回收、回收、回收、回收、回收、回收、回收 。
whenever possible , refuse singleuse and disposable plastics .	然而 , 假如 , 拒絕單一的塑膠 。
alternatives exist ; some of them are very oldschool .	替代性存在 ; 有些人非常古老的選擇 。
i myself am now collecting these cool pyrex containers and using those instead of glad and tupperware containers to store food in .	我現在正在收集這些酷炫的精神保持這些酷兒 , 而不是玻璃 , 而是用玻璃來儲存食物 。
and i know that i am doing a service to myself and my family .	我知道 , 我在做一個服務給自己和家人 。
it's very easy to pick up a stainlesssteel bottle or a glass bottle , if you're traveling and you've forgotten to bring your stainlesssteel bottle and fill that up with water or filtered water , versus purchasing plastic bottled water .	很容易挑選一個無限的瓶子 , 或是玻璃瓶 , 如果你旅行 , 你就忘記了 , 你忘記了 , 你忘記了水或水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、水、
i guess what i want to say to everybody here and i know that you guys know a lot about this issue is that this is a huge problem in the oceans , but this is a problem that we've created as consumers and we can solve .	我想跟大家說這問題 , 我知道你們在海洋中有很多關於這個議題 , 但這是我們在海洋中創造的大問題 , 但這是我們創建的消費者 , 我們可以解決 。
we can solve this by raising awareness of the issue and teaching people to choose alternatives .	我們可以透過議題來解決這個問題 , 並教導人們選擇選擇替代代代代方案 。
so whenever possible , to choose alternatives to singleuse plastics .	因此 , 選擇選擇替代塑膠 。
we can cut the stem tide the stem of this into our oceans and in doing so , save our oceans , save our planet , save ourselves .	我們可以把它切割成我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的地球 , 拯救我們的地球 , 拯救地球 , 拯救我們自己 。

i've been intrigued by this question of whether we could evolve or develop a sixth sense a sense that would give us seamless access and easy access to metainformation or information that may exist somewhere that may be relevant to help us make the right decision about whatever it is that we're coming across .	我一直被這個問題 , 不論我們是否能進化或開發一個六個感知 , 可以給我們看不見的資訊 , 或資訊可能存在某些地方 , 可以幫助我們做出正確的決策 , 來協助我們做出正確的決策 。

and so my research group at the media lab has been developing a series of inventions to give us access to this information in a sort of easy way , without requiring that the user changes any of their behavior .	所以我的研究團隊在媒體實驗室研發了一系列發明了一種簡單的方式 , 不管使用者來取得這些資訊 , 在使用者身上改變任何行為 。

phyllis rodriguez and aicha elwafi have a powerful friendship born of unthinkable loss . rodriguez' son was killed in the world trade center attacks on september 11 , 2001 ; elwafi's son zacarias moussaoui was convicted of a role in those attacks and is serving a life sentence . in hoping to find peace , these two moms have come to understand and respect one another .	phyllisrodriz和ichaelwafi有一個強大的朋友出生於世界貿易中心的攻擊 , 2001年11月11日 , 2001年11月11日 , 2001年 , 2001年 , 2001年 , 2001年 , 伊斯蘭克•摩爾•摩爾•摩爾•摩爾和平 , 找到了另一位媽媽媽媽媽媽媽 , 找到了另一位母親 。
culture , global issues , politics	文化、全球議題、政治議題 。
9/11 healing: the mothers who found forgiveness , friendship	9/11的亨利:那些找到認知、友誼、友誼、友誼 。
phyllis rodriguez: we are here today because of the fact that we have what most people consider an unusual friendship .	菲爾斯•羅德:我們今天這裡有許多人認為一個不尋常的友誼 。
and yet , it feels natural to us now .	然而 , 這感覺很自然地對我們來說很自然 。
i first learned that my son had been in the world trade center on the morning of september 11th , 2001 .	我第一次知道我的兒子已經在世界貿易中心 , 2001年11月11日 。
we didn't know if he had perished yet until 36 hours later .	我們不知道他是否有被告知 , 直到36小時後 。
at the time , we knew that it was political .	在那時 , 我們知道這是政治 。
we were afraid of what our country was going to do in the name of our son my husband , orlando , and i and our family .	我們對我們的國家的名字是害怕我們的兒子 , 或土地 , 我和我的家人 。
and when i saw it and yet , through the shock , the terrible shock , and the terrible explosion in our lives , literally , we were not vengeful .	當我看到它 , 震驚時 , 我驚訝的是 , 很糟糕的爆炸 , 真的 , 我們生活在生活中 , 真的 , 我們沒有太幸運了 。
and a couple of weeks later when zacarias moussaoui was indicted on six counts of conspiracy to commit terrorism , and the u . s . government called for a death penalty for him , if convicted , my husband and i spoke out in opposition to that , publicly .	幾週後 , 當ziamoussaoui被注意到 , 六個數目後 , 美國政府稱之為死刑的恐怖主義 , 美國政府稱之為死刑 , 如果保守了 , 我的丈夫 , 我和丈夫 。
through that and through human rights groups , we were brought together with several other victims' families .	透過人類權利團體 , 我們和其他受害者一起合作 。
when i saw aicha in the media , coming over when her son was indicted , and i thought , " what a brave woman .	當我在媒體上看到阿根廷時 , 在她兒子被注意到: 「 勇敢的女人 。 」
someday i want to meet that woman when i'm stronger . "	有一天 , 我想要見到那個女人的時候 。 」
i was still in deep grief ; i knew i didn't have the strength .	我仍然在深悲傷 , 我知道我沒有力量 。
i knew i would find her someday , or we would find each other .	我知道我會找到她的日子 , 或者我們會找到彼此 。
because , when people heard that my son was a victim , i got immediate sympathy .	因為當人們聽到我的兒子是受害者 , 我得到立刻的對象 。
but when people learned what her son was accused of , she didn't get that sympathy .	但當人們知道她的兒子是什麼 , 她沒有得到這對象 。
but her suffering is equal to mine .	但她的苦難是平等的 。
so we met in november 2002 , and aicha will now tell you how that came about .	所以我們在2002年11月2日 , 阿拉罕會告訴各位 , 這是怎麼回事 。

for all the women , all the mothers that give life , you can give back , you can change .	對所有婦女來說 , 所有的母親 , 你可以回復 , 你可以回復 。

pr: i would like to say that i have learned so much from aicha , starting with that day we had our very first meeting with other family members which was a very private meeting with security , because it was november 2002 , and , frankly , we were afraid of the superpatriotism of that time in the country those of us family members .	帕爾:我想說我從阿根廷學到了很多 , 從那天開始 , 我們的家庭成員 , 這是非常私人的成員 , 因為這不是2002年11月2002日 , 坦白說 , 我們是害怕的超級恐怖主義 。

so nothing is getting through .	所以 , 什麼都沒有通過 。

paddy ashdown claims that we are living in a moment in history where power is changing in ways it never has before . in a spellbinding talk at tedxbrussels he outlines the three major global shifts that he sees coming .	悲傷的是 , 我們在歷史上生活的時刻 , 力量正在改變它從未有過過的時刻 , 在tedxbrusel的演講中 , 他從來沒有過過過的三個主要全球轉變 。

paddy ashdown: the global power shift	幸運的是 , 全球權力轉變 。
there's a poem written by a very famous english poet at the end of the 19th century .	在19世紀末末 , 有一首詩的英文詩 , 在19世紀末末 ,

and the poem goes: " on the idle hill of summer , lazy with the flow of streams , hark i hear a distant drummer , drumming like a sound in dreams , far and near and low and louder on the roads of earth go by , dear to friend and food to powder , soldiers marching , soon to die . "	詩人說: 「 在夏天 , 我和夏天的流動 , 笑著我聽過一個遙遠的飲料 , 我聽到一個遙遠的戲劇 , 降低地球的路徑 , 穿著地球的路線上 , 沙漠 , 士兵和食物的路徑 。 」
those who are interested in poetry , the poem is " a shropshire lad " written by a . e . housman .	這些人對詩人感到興趣 , 詩是 「 商店 」 , 詩人 」 寫著 「 店 」 寫作 。
but what housman understood , and you hear it in the symphonies of nielsen too , was that the long , hot , silvan summers of stability of the 19th century were coming to a close , and that we were about to move into one of those terrifying periods of history when power changes .	但在19世紀時 , 你也聽到它 , 在尼爾森也聽到它 , 長久以來 , 是長期、熱情、熱情、熱情、熱情的夏天 , 我們要搬進過去的一步 , 當我們改變歷史的歷史 。
and these are always periods , ladies and gentlemen , accompanied by turbulence , and all too often by blood .	這些都是永久的 , 女士們、女士、女士、女士、女士 , 都被血液 。
and my message for you is that i believe we are condemned , if you like , to live at just one of those moments in history when the gimbals upon which the established order of power is beginning to change and the new look of the world , the new powers that exist in the world , are beginning to take form .	我的訊息是 , 我相信我們被關心的 , 如果你喜歡 , 只要你活在歷史上最高的一刻 , 就會開始改變世界的力量就是開始改變世界的新力量就是開始改變世界的新勢力 。
and these are and we see it very clearly today nearly always highly turbulent times , highly difficult times , and all too often very bloody times .	這些都是今天我們看到的 , 很明顯地 , 幾乎是非常困難的次數 , 而且常常常常常非常血腥 。
by the way , it happens about once every century .	順便一提 , 每世紀都發生了 。
you might argue that the last time it happened and that's what housman felt coming and what churchill felt too was that when power passed from the old nations , the old powers of europe , across the atlantic to the new emerging power of the united states of america the beginning of the american century .	你可能會說 , 最後一次它發生了什麼事 , 那就是在古老國家的感受和教堂一樣 , 當歐洲從古老國家開始 , 到歐洲 , 在大西洋的新興力量 , 到美國世紀初 , 美國世紀初期的力量 。
and of course , into the vacuum where the tooold european powers used to be were played the two bloody catastrophes of the last century the one in the first part and the one in the second part: the two great world wars .	當然 , 在過去的世紀中 , 歐洲權力已經扮演了兩個血腥災難 , 第二個世紀初 , 第二部分是:兩個偉大的戰爭 。
mao zedong used to refer to them as the european civil wars , and it's probably a more accurate way of describing them .	馬里曾曾被迫害到歐洲公民戰爭 , 可能更加準確的方式描述他們 。
well , ladies and gentlemen , we live at one of those times .	嗯 , 女士們 , 我們住在這些時代 。
but for us , i want to talk about three factors today .	但對我們來說 , 我想談三個因素 。
and the first of these , the first two of these , is about a shift in power .	這些 , 首先 , 這是權力的轉變 。
and the second is about some new dimension which i want to refer to , which has never quite happened in the way it's happening now .	第二個是關於一些新的方向 , 我想重新設計師 , 這從來沒有發生在發生的事情中發生 。
but let's talk about the shifts of power that are occurring to the world .	但我們來談談這個權力改變世界的改變 。
and what is happening today is , in one sense , frightening because it's never happened before .	今天發生的是 , 在某種意義上 , 因為它從未發生過的事 。
we have seen lateral shifts of power the power of greece passed to rome and the power shifts that occurred during the european civilizations but we are seeing something slightly different .	後來我們看到希臘的力量轉變為羅馬和權力轉移到羅馬和權力轉變 , 但我們看到了一些事情 。
for power is not just moving laterally from nation to nation .	權力不僅僅從國家搬到國家 。
it's also moving vertically .	它也正在移動 。
what's happening today is that the power that was encased , held to accountability , held to the rule of law , within the institution of the nation state has now migrated in very large measure onto the global stage .	今天發生的是 , 國內的力量 , 他告訴了法律 , 他告訴法律的規則 , 在全球階段中 , 在非常大的測量 , 在全球階段中 , 在非常大量測量全球階段 。
the globalization of power we talk about the globalization of markets , but actually it's the globalization of real power .	我們談到市場的力量 , 但事實上這是真實力量的全球化化化 。
and where , at the nation state level that power is held to accountability subject to the rule of law , on the international stage it is not .	在那裡 , 在國家層面上 , 權力是他要求法律 , 國際舞台上 , 國際舞台上並不一樣 。
the international stage and the global stage where power now resides: the power of the internet , the power of the satellite broadcasters , the power of the money changers this vast moneygoround that circulates now 32 times the amount of money necessary for the trade it's supposed to be there to finance the money changers , if you like , the financial speculators that have brought us all to our knees quite recently , the power of the multinational corporations now developing budgets often bigger than mediumsized countries .	國際舞台和全球舞台的力量:網路、衛星、衛星、衛星、銀行、金錢改變這些巨大的金錢改變 , 現在的貨幣的力量 , 將錢轉換成32倍 。
these live in a global space which is largely unregulated , not subject to the rule of law , and in which people may act free of constraint .	這些生活在一個全球空間中 , 不管是法律的規則 , 而在那些人可能自由的規則 。
now that suits the powerful up to a moment .	現在 , 突然間有強大的力量 。
it's always suitable for those who have the most power to operate in spaces without constraint , but the lesson of history is that , sooner or later , unregulated space space not subject to the rule of law becomes populated , not just by the things you wanted international trade , the internet , etc . but also by the things you don't want international criminality , international terrorism .	總是永續貿易的那些擁有最權力的人 , 但歷史上 , 不論歷史上最快的空間 , 但歷史上 , 不管是你想要國際貿易空間的規則 , 不只是你想要國際貿易、網際貿易、網際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易、國際貿易 。
the revelation of 9/11 is that even if you are the most powerful nation on earth , nevertheless , those who inhabit that space can attack you even in your most iconic of cities one bright september morning .	911事件是 , 即使你是地球上最強大的國家 , 除非 , 除非 , 除非 , 那些在你大部分城市中最強大的城市 。
it's said that something like 60 percent of the four million dollars that was taken to fund 9/11 actually passed through the institutions of the twin towers which 9/11 destroyed .	它說 , 大約有百分之六十的錢是為了資助機構資助機構的機構 , 91111事件被摧毀了 。
you see , our enemies also use this space the space of mass travel , the internet , satellite broadcasters to be able to get around their poison , which is about destroying our systems and our ways .	你知道嗎 , 我們的敵人也使用這個空間空間 , 網路、衛星、衛星、衛星、衛星、衛星、網路、我們的方式 。
sooner or later , sooner or later , the rule of history is that where power goes governance must follow .	不久之後 , 歷史學家或之後 , 歷史的規則是 , 權力的規則必須遵循 。
and if it is therefore the case , as i believe it is , that one of the phenomenon of our time is the globalization of power , then it follows that one of the challenges of our time is to bring governance to the global space .	如果這是我相信這是我們時代的一個現象之一 , 我相信這是我們時間的全球化力量之一 , 然後它遵循全球化空間的挑戰之一之一 , 然後它遵循全球空間的挑戰之一 。
and i believe that the decades ahead of us now will be to a greater or lesser extent turbulent the more or less we are able to achieve that aim: to bring governance to the global space .	我相信 , 十年來 , 我們現在將會成為更大或更少的外科手術 , 或是我們能達到這個目標:把金融到全球空間空間中 。
now notice , i'm not talking about government .	注意到 , 我不是在談論政府 。
i'm not talking about setting up some global democratic institution .	我不是在談論建立一些全球民主機構 。
my own view , by the way , ladies and gentlemen , is that this is unlikely to be done by spawning more u . n . institutions .	我自己的觀點來看 , 女士們們 , 就是這真的很不可思議 。

the world needs an international forum .	世界需要一個國際消費者 。
it needs a means by which you can legitimize international action .	它需要一個意義的意思是 , 你可以合法化國際行動 。
but when it comes to governance of the global space , my guess is this won't happen through the creation of more u . n . institutions .	但當它來到全球空間時 , 我的猜測不是透過更多美國創意的創意 。
it will actually happen by the powerful coming together and making treatybased systems , treatybased agreements , to govern that global space .	它會是由強大的聚集在一起 , 以治療基礎基礎的系統 , 去治癒這個全球空間 。
and if you look , you can see them happening , already beginning to emerge .	如果你看 , 你可以看到他們正在發生 , 已經開始擁抱 。
the world trade organization: treatybased organization , entirely treatybased , and yet , powerful enough to hold even the most powerful , the united states , to account if necessary .	世界貿易組織:治療基於治療的組織 , 但強大到美國 , 足夠強大 , 即使有必要的必要 。

the g20: we know now that we have to put together an institution which is capable of bringing governance to that financial space for financial speculation .	g20:我們現在知道 , 我們必須把金融機構放在金融空間中 。
and that's what the g20 is , a treatybased institution .	這就是g2020年 , 一個治療基礎的基礎 。
now there's a problem there , and we'll come back to it in a minute , which is that if you bring the most powerful together to make the rules in treatybased institutions , to fill that governance space , then what happens to the weak who are left out ?	現在有一個問題 , 我們會回到它 , 在一分鐘內 , 如果你把最強大的機構結合在一起 , 那就算你把最強大的機構放在一起 , 去填補那個西方太空船 , 那麼弱點會發生什麼事 ?
and that's a big problem , and we'll return to it in just a second .	這是個很大的問題 , 我們會回顧一下一下 。
so there's my first message , that if you are to pass through these turbulent times more or less turbulently , then our success in doing that will in large measure depend on our capacity to bring sensible governance to the global space .	所以 , 我的第一個訊息是 , 如果你通過這些外科手術 , 那麼我們成功的成功 , 那麼我們成功的成功 , 我們成功地在大量的目標上 , 將成功地帶到全球空間中 。
and watch that beginning to happen .	看看那一開始發生 。
my second point is , and i know i don't have to talk to an audience like this about such a thing , but power is not just shifting vertically , it's also shifting horizontally .	我的第二點是 , 我知道我不需要跟像這樣的觀眾談話 , 但權力並不只是轉變 。
you might argue that the story , the history of civilizations , has been civilizations gathered around seas with the first ones around the mediterranean , the more recent ones in the ascendents of western power around the atlantic .	你可能會說故事 , 文明歷史文明的歷史歷史歷史 , 一直在文明中 , 有文明的第一件事 , 在西方的西方國家 , 越近西洋棋 。
well it seems to me that we're now seeing a fundamental shift of power , broadly speaking , away from nations gathered around the atlantic [seaboard] to the nations gathered around the pacific rim .	這似乎對我來說 , 我們現在看到了一個基本元素、廣泛地說話 , 從國際大西洋上 , 從國際大西洋的國家聚集在一起 。
now that begins with economic power , but that's the way it always begins .	現在這一切從經濟力量開始 , 但這一切總是開始 。
you already begin to see the development of foreign policies , the augmentation of military budgets occurring in the other growing powers in the world .	你已經開始看到外國政策、軍事預算 , 在其他成長過程中 , 你已經開始在其他成長的力量 。
i think actually this is not so much a shift from the west to the east ; something different is happening .	我認為這並不是從西方到東岸的轉變 , 不同的發生 。
my guess is , for what it's worth , is that the united states will remain the most powerful nation on earth for the next 10 years , 15 , but the context in which she holds her power has now radically altered ; it has radically changed .	我的猜測是 , 對美國而言 , 美國會維持最強大的國家將會維持最強大的國家 , 但她在未來十年內 , 她把她的權力放在權力上 。
we are coming out of 50 years , most unusual years , of history in which we have had a totally monopolar world , in which every compass needle for or against has to be referenced by its position to washington a world bestrode by a single colossus .	我們從五十年來 , 大部分的歷史中 , 歷史上我們必須完全現代世界各地的歷史 , 都需要釋放或對抗華盛頓世界最好的英雄 。
but that's not a usual case in history .	但這不是一個典型的例子 。
in fact , what's now emerging is the much more normal case of history .	事實上 , 現在 , 現代歷史更正常的例子 。
you're beginning to see the emergence of a multipolar world .	你開始看到多種文化世界的力量 。
up until now , the united states has been the dominant feature of our world .	直到現在 , 美國是世界上最大的特徵 。

europe in the 19th century: a great british foreign secretary , lord canning , used to describe it as the " european concert of powers . "	19世紀 , 在19世紀 , 一個偉大的英國秘密 , 倫敦可以描述它為 「 歐洲保證 」 。
there was a balance , a fivesided balance .	有一種平衡 , 一個平衡的平衡 。
britain always played to the balance .	英國總是扮演平衡 。
if paris got together with berlin , britain got together with vienna and rome to provide a counterbalance .	如果巴黎和柏林一起一起合作 , 英國和羅馬一起合作 , 要提供一個更平衡 。
now notice , in a period which is dominated by a monopolar world , you have fixed alliances nato , the warsaw pact .	注意到 , 在一個永久的世界中 , 被一個月球的世界中 , 你已經被解決了所有人工智慧的太空船 。
a fixed polarity of power means fixed alliances .	一個固定的權力意味著固定的所有技能 。
but a multiple polarity of power means shifting and changing alliances .	但有許多權力的力量意味著轉變和改變平衡 。
and that's the world we're coming into , in which we will increasingly see that our alliances are not fixed .	這就是我們正在進入這個世界中 , 我們將會非常明顯地看到我們的平衡並不是被解決的 。
canning , the great british foreign secretary once said , " britain has a common interest , but no common allies . "	可以否否認 , 偉大的英國秘密曾說: 「 英國有共同點 」 。

my guess is iraq and afghanistan are the last times when the west has tried to do it themselves , and we haven't succeeded .	我的猜測是伊拉克和阿富汗是最後一次當西方的最後一次 , 我們沒有成功 。
my guess is that we're reaching the beginning of the end of 400 years i say 400 years because it's the end of the ottoman empire of the hegemony of western power , western institutions and western values .	我的猜測是 , 我們在400年結束後 , 我說400年來 , 因為它是蘇曼帝國的末端 , 西方機構的終點 , 西方機構和西方價值觀 。
you know , up until now , if the west got its act together , it could propose and dispose in every corner of the world .	直到現在 , 直到現在 , 如果我們把它結合在一起 , 它就能提議和全世界各個角落 。

i suspect we are now reaching the end of 400 years when western power was enough .	我猜我們現在已經到達400年了 , 當西方權力已經夠了 。

they want to keep the sea lanes open .	他們想要保持海層開放 。
increasingly , we are going to have to do business with people with whom we do not share values , but with whom , for the moment , we share common interests .	令人驚訝的是 , 我們要和那些我們不分享價值觀的人 , 但在那一刻 , 我們分享共同的興趣 。

and here's the third factor , which is totally different .	這是第三個工廠 , 完全不同 。
today in our modern world , because of the internet , because of the kinds of things people have been talking about here , everything is connected to everything .	今天在我們的現代世界 , 因為網際網路 , 是因為人們一直在談論這件事 , 一切都連結到一切 。

and what that means is the idea of a nation state acting alone , not connected with others , not working with others , is no longer a viable proposition .	這意味著 , 國家行動獨自行動的概念 , 而不是與其他人合作 , 而不是與其他人合作 , 而是更久的建議 。
because the actions of a nation state are neither confined to itself , nor is it sufficient for the nation state itself to control its own territory , because the effects outside the nation state are now beginning to affect what happens inside them .	因為國家國家的行動行為行為 , 不管是國內國家本身 , 沒有效率 , 沒有效率 , 因為國外國家的效應 , 現在國家的效應 , 因為外國國家外的效應 , 現在正開始影響他們內部的影響 。
i was a young soldier in the last of the small empire wars of britain .	我是一位年輕士兵的最後一個年輕士兵的戰爭 。
at that time , the defense of my country was about one thing and one thing only: how strong was our army , how strong was our air force , how strong was our navy and how strong were our allies .	在那時候 , 我的國家是大約一件事 , 只有一件事:我們的軍隊 , 我們的軍隊 , 強烈是我們的軍隊 , 以及我們的軍隊 。
that was when the enemy was outside the walls .	那就是當敵人在牆壁外外面 。
now the enemy is inside the walls .	敵人在牆壁裡 。
now if i want to talk about the defense of my country , i have to speak to the minister of health because pandemic disease is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of agriculture because food security is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of industry because the fragility of our hitech infrastructure is now a point of attack for our enemies as we see from cyber warfare i have to speak to the minister of home affairs because who has entered my country , who lives in that terraced house in that inner city has a direct effect on what happens in my country as we in london saw in the 7/7 bombings .	現在 , 如果我想要談我的國家 , 我必須和健康談話 , 我必須跟我說話 , 因為心理疾病是一種威脅 , 我必須跟我說話 , 因為食物安全是一種威脅 , 因為食物安全是一種威脅的威脅 , 我必須跟我說話 , 因為食物安全是一種威脅是我的國家 , 我必須跟我們談到的基礎建設 。
it's no longer the case that the security of a country is simply a matter for its soldiers and its ministry of defense .	它不再是國家安全安全的案例 , 僅僅僅僅僅僅是軍隊的重要性 。
it's its capacity to lock together its institutions .	它是有能力將它鎖起來 。
and this tells you something very important .	這告訴你們一些非常重要的事 。
it tells you that , in fact , our governments , vertically constructed , constructed on the economic model of the industrial revolution vertical hierarchy , specialization of tasks , command structures have got the wrong structures completely .	它告訴你們 , 事實上 , 我們的政府、政府、建構、工業革命、工業革命、工業革命的經濟模式 。
you in business know that the paradigm structure of our time , ladies and gentlemen , is the network .	你知道 , 在我們的時間中 , 女士和女士的結構結構結構結構 。
