the brightest spot in china , which you can see on the edge of the outline here , is hong kong .	在中國最聰明的地點 , 你可以在網路上看到的那邊 , 是香港的 。
hong kong was a small bit of china that , for most of the 20th century , operated under a very different set of rules than the rest of mainland china rules that were copied from working market economies of the time , and administered by the british .	荷蘭卡是一個中國大部份的中國 , 大部分的規則 , 在一個非常不同的規則 , 比主要中國的國家經濟規則 , 由英國的經濟規則 , 由英國政策的國家經濟規則 。
in the 1950s , hong kong was a place where millions of people could go , from the mainland , to start in jobs like sewing shirts , making toys .	在1950年 , 荷蘭卡地區有數百萬人可以從主要的土地開始 , 從主要的角落開始 。
but , to get on a process of increasing income , increasing skills led to very rapid growth there .	但 , 為了收入收入的過程中 , 讓技能變得非常快速成長 。
hong kong was also the model which leaders like deng xiaoping could copy , when they decided to move all of the mainland towards the market model .	荷蘭卡也也是領導者一樣的模型 , 當他們決定搬到市場模型時 , 當他們決定搬到市場模型時 , 最主要的陸地向前邁進 。
but deng xiaoping instinctively understood the importance of offering choices to his people .	但深刻地了解他人的重要性 , 要選擇他人的重要性 。
so instead of forcing everyone in china to shift immediately to the market model , they proceeded by creating some special zones that could do , in a sense , what britain did: make the opportunity to go work with the market rules available to the people who wanted to opt in there .	所以 , 不是為了根據中國來改變市場模式 , 他們被創造出一些特別的zone模型 , 他們被創造出一些特別的zone , 英國做的機會:讓機會和市場規則合作 , 讓機會和市場規則合作 。
so they created four special economic zones around hong kong: zones where chinese could come and work , and cities grew up very rapidly there ; also zones where foreign firms could come in and make things .	所以他們創造了四個特殊的經濟zones:zonezone在那裡 , 中國長大 , 還有城市長大 , 城市長大 , 還有zoneszones可以來到那裡 。
one of the zones next to hong kong has a city called shenzhen .	下一到荷蘭的一座城市之一 , 叫做她nzhenzhen 。
in that city there is a taiwanese firm that made the iphone that many of you have , and they made it with labor from chinese who moved there to shenzhen .	在那座城市裡有一個目標 , 讓許多人擁有的iphone , 他們從中國搬到她搬到那兒搬到她去那裡 。
so after the four special zones , there were 14 coastal cites that were open in the same sense , and eventually demonstrated successes in these places that people could opt in to , that they flocked to because of the advantages they offered .	所以在四個特殊的zone後 , 有14個共同點 , 最終在這些地方開放成功的成功 , 最終 , 人們可以在這些地方逃離成功的成功 , 因為他們提供了優勢的優勢 。
demonstrated successes there led to a consensus for a move toward the market model for the entire economy .	展示了成功的成功 , 導致整個經濟模式 , 讓整個經濟模式轉向整個經濟模式 。
now the chinese example shows us several points .	現在中國的例子顯示了我們數個點 。
one is: preserve choices for people .	第一:為人們保存選擇 。
two: operate on the right scale .	第二:在右邊的右邊 。
if you try to change the rules in a village , you could do that , but a village would be too small to get the kinds of benefits you can get if you have millions of people all working under good rules .	如果你試著改變村莊裡的規則 , 你可以這樣做 , 但村莊可能會太小 , 但村莊會太小了 , 你可以得到數百萬人都在好規則中工作 。
on the other hand , the nation is too big .	另一方面 , 國家太大了 。
if you try to change the rules in the nation , you can't give some people a chance to hold back , see how things turn out , and let others zoom ahead and try the new rules .	如果你試著改變國家的規則 , 你不能給一些機會 , 看看結果結果 , 看看結果是什麼結果 , 讓其他zo原則 , 嘗試新的規則 。
but cities give you this opportunity to create new places , with new rules that people can opt in to .	但城市給你一個機會創造新的地方 , 讓人們可以選擇去做新的規則 。
and they're large enough to get all of the benefits that we can have when millions of us work together under good rules .	他們很大 , 足以取得我們所能有的利益規則 。
so the proposal is that we conceive of something called a charter city .	所以我們的建議是 , 叫做 「 查爾市民 」 。
we start with a charter that specifies all the rules required to attract the people who we'll need to build the city .	我們從一個章節開始 , 所有規則需要吸引我們建造城市的人 。
we'll need to attract the investors who will build out the infrastructure the power system , the roads , the port , the airport , the buildings .	我們需要吸引力投資者的投資者 , 他們會建立在權力系統中建造出來的基礎建設 。
you'll need to attract firms , who will come hire the people who move there first .	你需要吸引力飛行器 , 他會僱用那些移動的人們 。
and you'll need to attract families , the residents who will come and live there permanently , raise their children , get an education for their children , and get their first job .	而你需要吸引家庭、家人 , 那些會來到那裡 , 居民地地 , 他們的孩子們 , 讓他們的第一份工作 。
with that charter , people will move there .	在那個章節中 , 人們會搬到那裡 。
the city can be built .	城市可以建造 。
and we can scale this model .	我們可以把這個模型放進這個模型 。
we can go do it over and over again .	我們可以再做一次 。
to make it work , we need good rules . we've already discussed that .	為了讓它運作 , 我們需要好的規則 。 我們已經討論了 。
those are captured in the charter .	這些都是在章節中捕捉到的 。
we also need the choices for people .	我們也需要對人來說選擇 。
that's really built into the model if we allow for the possibility of building cities on uninhabited land .	如果我們允許建造城市的可能性 , 如果我們允許建造城市的可能性 。
you start from uninhabited territory .	你從未知的恐怖分子開始 。
people can come live under the new charter , but no one is forced to live under it .	人們可以住在新的章節 , 但沒有人被迫害 。
the final thing we need are choices for leaders .	最後我們需要的是領導人的選擇 。
and , to achieve the kind of choices we want for leaders we need to allow for the potential for partnerships between nations: cases where nations work together , in effect , de facto , the way china and britain worked together to build , first a little enclave of the market model , and then scale it throughout china .	為了達到一個我們想要領導者的選擇 , 我們需要讓領導者之間的潛力:國家和英國和英國之間合作合作 , 事實上 , 中國和英國和英國合作 , 首先 , 首先 , 中國和英國和英國合作 。
in a sense , britain , inadvertently , through its actions in hong kong , did more to reduce world poverty than all the aid programs that we've undertaken in the last century .	某種程度上 , 英國、英國、英國、英國、更加減少世界貧窮的案例 , 不僅僅僅僅在過去世紀內 。
so if we allow for these kind of partnerships to replicate this again , we can get those kinds of benefits scaled throughout the world .	所以 , 如果我們允許這些合作夥伴重新複製這個世界 , 我們可以把這些類型的益處 。
in some cases this will involve a delegation of responsibility , a delegation of control from one country to another to take over certain kinds of administrative responsibilities .	在某些情況下 , 這會涉及責任的責任 , 從一個國家到另一種國家的控制能力 。
now , when i say that , some of you are starting to think , " well , is this just bringing back colonialism ? "	當我說這句話時 , 有些人開始想: 「 嗯 , 這只是帶回殖民主義 ? 」
it's not . but it's important to recognize that the kind of emotions that come up when we start to think about these things , can get in the way , can make us pull back , can shut down our ability , and our interest in trying to explore new ideas .	這不是 。 但很重要的是要了解這些東西 , 當我們開始思考這些東西時 , 我們就能把這些東西放回我們的能力 , 可以讓我們回去探索新想法 , 可以讓我們回到我們的能力 , 我們的興趣 。
why is this not like colonialism ?	為什麼不喜歡殖民主義 ?
the thing that was bad about colonialism , and the thing which is residually bad in some of our aid programs , is that it involved elements of coercion and condescension .	對於殖民主義而言 , 事情很糟糕的是 , 在我們的一些援助計畫中 , 它涉及了認知的元素和認知 。
this model is all about choices , both for leaders and for the people who will live in these new places .	這模型是關於領導人和領導人 , 兩者都住在這些新地方 。
and , choice is the antidote to coercion and condescension .	選擇是抗議和認知 。
so let's talk about how this could play out in practice .	讓我們來談談這怎麼能在練習中演奏 。
let's take a particular leader , raul castro , who is the leader of cuba .	咱們來舉個特別領導者 , 他是阿根廷的領導者 。
it must have occurred to castro that he has the chance to do for cuba what deng xiaoping did for china , but he doesn't have a hong kong there on the island in cuba .	這一定一定會發生發生 , 他有機會去拯救中國的危險 , 但他沒有一個月球 , 但他沒有一個熱帶的肯亞 。
he does , though , have a little bit of light down in the south that has a very special status .	不過 , 南南邊有一點光光線的光線 。
there is a zone there , around guantanamo bay , where a treaty gives the united states administrative responsibility for a piece of land that's about twice the size of manhattan .	那裡有一個zonezone , 南亞的巴士 , 一個治療師給美國大陸的責任 , 對於曼哈頓的兩倍大 。
castro goes to the prime minister of canada and says , " look , the yankees have a terrible pr problem .	克里斯登到加拿拿拿大 , 然後說: 「 看看 , yankeke有一個很糟糕的問題 。
they want to get out .	他們想要脫離 。
why don't you , canada , take over ?	為什麼你不 , 加拿大 , 拿大 ?
build run a special administrative zone .	建造一個特殊的礦坑 。
allow a new city to be built up there .	讓一個新的城市建立起來 。
allow many people to come in .	讓許多人進來 。
let us have a hong kong nearby .	咱們來看看附近的韓國 。
some of my citizens will move into that city as well .	我有些公民會搬進那座城市 。
others will hold back . but this will be the gateway that will connect the modern economy and the modern world to my country . "	其他人會再回來 , 但這將會成為現代經濟和現代世界 , 和現代的世界 。 」
now , where else might this model be tried ?	現在 , 其他的模型可能在哪裡 ?
well , africa . i've talked with leaders in africa .	非洲 , 我和領導人談到非洲 。
many of them totally get the notion of a special zone that people can opt into as a rule .	許多人都無法選擇一個特殊的謎題 , 人們無法選擇成為一個規則 。
it's a rule for changing rules .	這是一個改變規則 。
it's a way to create new rules , and let people optin without coercion , and the opposition that coercion can force .	這是一種方法來創造新的規則 , 讓人們選擇沒有合作 , 而不是合作 , 而是合作的相反 。
they also totally get the idea that in some instances they can make more credible promises to longterm investors the kind of investors who will come build the port , build the roads , in a new city they can make more credible promises if they do it along with a partner nation .	他們也知道 , 在某些例子中 , 他們也能讓更多驚人的承諾 , 他們能創造更多的投資者 , 他們能創造更多的投資者 , 建立新的城市 , 如果他們和一個合作夥伴 , 建立更可思議的承諾 。
perhaps even in some arrangement that's a little bit like an escrow account , where you put land in the escrow account and the partner nation takes responsibility for it .	也許在某些論點中 , 有點像一個帳戶一樣 , 你把土地放進帳戶裡 , 你把土地放進去 。
there is also lots of land in africa where new cities could be built .	非洲還有很多很多島嶼 , 新城市可以建立建構 。
this is a picture i took when i was flying along the coast .	這張照片是我在海岸飛行的照片 。
there are immense stretches of land like this land where hundreds of millions of people could live .	像這樣的島嶼 , 像這樣的島嶼 , 數百萬人能活下來 。
now , if we generalize this and think about not just one or two charter cites , but dozens cities that will help create places for the many hundreds of millions , perhaps billions of people who will move to cities in the coming century is there enough land for them ?	現在 , 如果我們一般化化這一點 , 想想不僅僅是2公里的城市 , 而是數十億人 , 也許有數十億人 , 或許有足夠的城市 , 或許有足夠的土地 , 也許有足夠的城市 ?
well , throughout the world , if we look at the lights at night , the one thing that's misleading is that , visually , it looks like most of the world is already built out .	嗯 , 在整個世界裡 , 如果我們仔細觀察光的光線 , 視覺上 , 通常 , 它看起來像世界上大部分已經建造出來了 。
so let me show you why that's wrong .	所以 , 讓我告訴你為什麼這是錯的 。
take this representation of all of the land .	拿這代表所有陸地的代表 。
turn it into a square that stands for all the arable land on earth .	轉換為地球上所有穩定的土地上 。
and let these dots represent the land that's already taken up by the cities that three billion people now live in .	咱們來代表這三十億人住在城市裡的城市 , 讓這三十億人住在城市裡 。
if you move the dots down to the bottom of the rectangle you can see that the cities for the existing three billion urban residents take up only three percent of the arable land on earth .	如果你搬到地球上的右邊 , 你可以看到 , 在地球上有三十億個城市復甦的城市 , 只剩三十億城市的居民 。
so if we wanted to build cities for another billion people , they would be dots like this .	所以如果我們想要建立城市 , 他們會這樣做 。
we'd go from three percent of the arable land , to four percent .	我們從三分之三的島嶼 , 到4% 。
we'd dramatically reduce the human footprint on earth by building more cities that people can move to .	我們很戲劇地減少人類足跡的城市 , 建造更多城市 , 讓人們搬到地球上 。
and if these are cities governed by good rules , they can be cities where people are safe from crime , safe from disease and bad sanitation , where people have a chance to get a job .	如果這些城市是良好的規則 , 它們可以從犯罪、安全的城市 , 人們有機會從犯罪、安全和壞衛生機構 , 人們有機會能得到工作 。
they can get basic utilities like electricity .	他們可以得到基本的能力 。
their kids can get an education .	他們的孩子可以得到教育 。
so what will it take to get started building the first charter cities , scaling this so we build many more ?	所以 , 我們要怎麼開始建造出第一章章章章魚 , 把這類城市建造更多呢 ?
it would help to have a manual .	它可以幫助一個人工智慧 。
what university professors could do is write some details that might go into this manual .	大學教授可以做的是寫一些細節可以寫一些細節的細節
you wouldn't want to let us run the cities , go out and design them .	你不想讓我們跑出城市 , 去設計城市 , 去設計它們 。
you wouldn't let academics out in the wild .	你不會讓學術界從野生開始 。
but , you could set us to work thinking about questions like , suppose it isn't just canada that does the deal with raul castro .	但 , 你可以讓我們思考問題像這樣的問題 , 假設它不只能加拿大火災 。
perhaps brazil comes in as a participant , and spain as well . and perhaps cuba wants to be one of the partners in a fourway joint venture .	也許巴西是參與者的參與者 , 也許是巴西想要成為四公里的夥伴之一之一 。
how would we write the treaty to do that ?	我們要如何寫這個治療方法來做這件事 ?
there is less precedent for that , but that could easily be worked out .	對此來說 , 沒有預防 , 但這可以容易成功 。
how would we finance this ?	我們要如何定義這個 ?
turns out singapore and hong kong are cities that made huge gains on the value of the land that they owned when they got started .	結果發現 , 加坡和荷蘭卡的城市價值 , 讓他們自己開始的時候 , 他們在他們開始的時候 。
you could use the gains on the value of the land to pay for things like the police , the courts , but the school system and the health care system too , which make this a more attractive place to live , makes this a place where people have higher incomes which , incidentally , makes the land more valuable .	你可以用在土地上使用玻璃的價值觀 , 但學校系統和健康照護系統的價值觀 , 讓學校和健康照護系統 , 讓這個地方變得更有趣 , 讓人們更有價值的收入 , 讓土地更有價值 。
so the incentives for the people helping to construct this zone and build it , and set up the basic rules , go very much in the right direction .	所以 , 對人們幫助建構這個zonetruct這個zone , 建立了基本規則 , 設定基本規則 , 以正確方向的方式來建構它 。
so there are many other details like this .	所以有許多其他細節的細節 。
how could we have buildings that are low cost and affordable for people who work in a first job , assembling something like an iphone , but make those buildings energy efficient , and make sure that they are safe , so they don't fall down in an earthquake or a hurricane .	我們要如何建造出這些是低成本和負擔負擔的人 , 如iphone , 但讓這些建築物更安全 , 但讓這些建築物更安全 , 確保它們是安全的 , 所以確保它們是安全的 , 所以他們不在地震或颶風 。
many technical details to be worked out , but those of us who are already starting to pursue these things can already tell that there is no roadblock , there's no impediment , other than a failure of imagination , that will keep us from delivering on a truly global winwin solution .	許多科技細節的細節 , 但這些人已經開始追求這些東西已經開始追求這些東西已經沒有辦法解決想像力 , 還沒有預料 , 其他的想像力 , 這將會讓我們從全球贏得全球贏得的解決方案 。
let me conclude with this picture .	讓我跟這張照片結論 。
the reason we can be so well off , even though there is so many people on earth , is because of the power of ideas .	原因我們可以很好 , 即使有許多人在地球上有很多人的力量 , 就是是因為想法的力量 。
we can share ideas with other people , and when they discover them , they share with us .	我們可以和其他人分享想法時 , 當他們發現他們與我們分享他們分享他們 。
it's not like scarce objects , where sharing means we each get less .	這不像害怕物體 , 分享意味著我們每一件事都比較少 。
when we share ideas we all get more .	當我們分享想法時 , 我們都變得越來越多 。
when we think about ideas in that way , we usually think about technologies .	當我們思考這個想法時 , 我們通常會想到科技科技科技 。
but there is another class of ideas: the rules that govern how we interact with each other ; rules like , let's have a tax system that supports a research university that gives away certain kinds of knowledge for free .	但還有另一個想法: 「 金融系統 」 規則我們如何與彼此互動 ; 例如 , 讓我們有一個稅系統 , 支持一個研究免費的系統 , 提供一些知識免費的知識 。
let's have a system where we have ownership of land that is registered in a government office , that people can pledge as collateral .	讓我們有一個系統 , 我們擁有權利的系統 , 就是在政府辦公室裡 , 人們可以把身為大學當作大學 。
if we can keep innovating on our space of rules , and particularly innovate in the sense of coming up with rules for changing rules , so we don't get stuck with bad rules , then we can keep moving progress forward and truly make the world a better place , so that people like nelson and his friends don't have to study any longer under the streetlights . thank you .	如果我們能保持創新的空間 , 尤其是創新規則 , 特別是改變規則 , 所以我們不能用壞規則 , 所以我們不能用壞規則 , 讓世界更好的規則 , 讓世界變得更好 , 所以人們像尼爾遜和朋友們一樣 。
genomics pioneer craig venter takes a break from his epic roundtheworld expedition to talk about the millions of genes his team has discovered so far in its quest to map the ocean’s biodiversity .	基因組專業專業的專業 , 從他的職業界的突破 , 來談談到海洋上百萬個基因多樣性 。
dna , biosphere , biotech , entrepreneur , genetics , invention , oceans , science , technology	dna、生物學、生物科技、企業家、企業家、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、科技、
craig venter on dna and the sea	爬上dna和海海海域 。
at the break , i was asked by several people about my comments about the aging debate .	在突破時 , 我被問過我的評論辯論 。
and this will be my only comment on it .	這將會是我唯一的信息 。
and that is , i understand that optimists greatly outlive pessimists .	這就是 , 我了解到 , 最樂觀主義者很擅長的心理學家 。
what i'm going to tell you about in my 18 minutes is how we're about to switch from reading the genetic code to the first stages of beginning to write the code ourselves .	我要告訴各位 , 在18分鐘內 , 就是我們如何從基因編寫基因編碼到第一個階段 , 來寫程式碼的第一階段 。
it's only 10 years ago this month when we published the first sequence of a freeliving organism , that of haemophilus influenzae .	只有10年前我們發佈了自由的第一部分 , 當我們發佈了免費生物體 , 包括哈大氣的影響 。
that took a genome project from 13 years down to four months .	那個基因組從13年到四個月 。
we can now do that same genome project in the order of two to eight hours .	現在我們可以做同樣的基因組計畫 , 兩到八個小時 。
so in the last decade , a large number of genomes have been added: most human pathogens , a couple of plants , several insects and several mammals , including the human genome .	所以在過去十年間 , 有許多基因組組都被加上了:大多數人類病原體 , 包括昆蟲和幾種哺乳類動物 , 包括人類基因組 。
genomics at this stage of the thinking from a little over 10 years ago was , by the end of this year , we might have between three and five genomes sequenced ; it's on the order of several hundred .	在十年前 , 基因組的過程中 , 我們可能有三到五個基因組 , 我們大概有三到五個基因組序列 ; 五個基因組序列 。
we just got a grant from the gordon and betty moore foundation to sequence 130 genomes this year , as a side project from environmental organisms .	我們一年從目標開始 , 從目標開始 , 每年有130個基因組組基金會 , 作為環境生物生物生物生物生物體 。
so the rate of reading the genetic code has changed .	所以閱讀基因編碼的速度已經改變了 。
but as we look , what's out there , we've barely scratched the surface on what is available on this planet .	但當我們觀察到的表面上 , 我們幾乎在地球表面上的表面 。
most people don't realize it , because they're invisible , but microbes make up about a half of the earth's biomass , whereas all animals only make up about one onethousandth of all the biomass .	大多數人並不了解 , 因為它們是很可見的 , 但微生物會讓地球上有大約一半的生物物 , 所有動物只能製造出1/3 。
and maybe it's something that people in oxford don't do very often , but if you ever make it to the sea , and you swallow a mouthful of seawater , keep in mind that each milliliter has about a million bacteria and on the order of 10 million viruses .	也許這是在奧克州的人們並不常常做的事 , 但如果你讓它到海水 , 你就會意識到一千萬個細菌 , 你就會意識到每毫毫毫米的細菌 , 保持每毫毫米病毒都有大約一億個細菌 。
less than 5 , 000 microbial species have been characterized as of two years ago , and so we decided to do something about it .	不到五千個微生物物種被視為兩年前 , 所以我們決定要做些什麼事 。
and we started the sorcerer ii expedition , where we were , as with great oceanographic expeditions , trying to sample the ocean every 200 miles .	我們開始了很恐怖的冰箱 , 我們正處於200英哩的地理 , 試著將海洋每200英哩 。
we started in bermuda for our test project , then moved up to halifax , working down the u . s . east coast , the caribbean sea , the panama canal , through to the galapagos , then across the pacific , and we're in the process now of working our way across the indian ocean .	我們從柏林開始 , 為我們的測試計畫 , 然後搬到美國海岸 , 加勒比海岸 , 加勒比海、加勒比海、加拿大、巴拿大、平洋 , 我們現在正在工作的過程 。
it's very tough duty ; we're doing this on a sailing vessel , in part to help excite young people about going into science .	非常艱難 , 我們正在做這個事 , 在一部分上 , 部分要幫助年輕人進入科學領域 。
the experiments are incredibly simple .	實驗是非常簡單 。
we just take seawater and we filter it , and we collect different size organisms on different filters , and then take their dna back to our lab in rockville , where we can sequence a hundred million letters of the genetic code every 24 hours .	我們只拿海水水池 , 我們收集不同的器官 , 我們收集不同的濾器 , 然後把他們的dna帶回我們的實驗室裡 , 我們可以把它們放到我們的實驗室裡 , 每24小時 。
and with doing this , we've made some amazing discoveries .	藉此做這件事 , 我們做了一些驚人的發現 。
for example , it was thought that the visual pigments that are in our eyes there was only one or two organisms in the environment that had these same pigments .	舉例來說 , 這是我們眼睛中的視覺圖案 , 只有1/2個生物體中只有兩種生物 。
it turns out , almost every species in the upper parts of the ocean in warm parts of the world have these same photoreceptors , and use sunlight as the source of their energy and communication .	結果發現 , 幾乎每種物種都在暖化的一部分都相同的攝影師 , 用太陽光和溝通 。
from one site , from one barrel of seawater , we discovered 1 . 3 million new genes and as many as 50 , 000 new species .	從一個地方開始 , 從一塊海水中 , 我們發現了1.3百萬個新基因 , 如同有50000個新物種 。
we've extended this to the air now with a grant from the sloan foundation .	我們現在已經擴展到空氣的基礎 。
we're measuring how many viruses and bacteria all of us are breathing in and out every day , particularly on airplanes or closed auditoriums .	我們正在追蹤多少病毒和細菌有關 , 每天都在呼吸中 , 特別是在飛機上 , 特別是在飛機上 , 特別是在飛機上 。
we filter through some simple apparatuses ; we collect on the order of a billion microbes from just a day filtering on top of a building in new york city .	我們透過一些簡單的顯微鏡 , 我們收集在紐約市裡收集了數十億微生物的數量 。
and we're in the process of sequencing all that at the present time .	我們在此刻 , 在現在的秘密過程中 ,
just on the data collection side , just where we are through the galapagos , we're finding that almost every 200 miles , we see tremendous diversity in the samples in the ocean .	只是在資料庫裡 , 我們發現 , 幾乎每200英哩 , 我們發現幾乎每200英哩 , 我們看到了很大的多樣性 。
some of these make logical sense , in terms of different temperature gradients .	有些有邏輯的感覺 , 在不同的溫度上 。
so this is a satellite photograph based on temperatures red being warm , blue being cold and we found there's a tremendous difference between the warm water samples and the cold water samples , in terms of abundant species .	這就是衛星攝影的衛星照片 , 根據溫度減少暖的溫度 , 藍色被冷卻 , 我們發現有很大的差異 。
the other thing that surprised us quite a bit is these photoreceptors detect different wavelengths of light , and we can predict that based on their amino acid sequence .	另外一件令人驚訝的是 , 這些照片的接受器官偵測不同的波長 , 我們可以預測光線上的不同波長 。
and these vary tremendously from region to region .	這些疫苗來自區域的區域 。
maybe not surprisingly , in the deep ocean , where it's mostly blue , the photoreceptors tend to see blue light .	也許不是令人驚訝的是 , 在深海海洋中 , 大部分藍色、攝影師通常會看到藍光 。
when there's a lot of chlorophyll around , they see a lot of green light .	當有許多英雄的圓圈時 , 他們看到很多綠光燈 。
but they vary even more , possibly moving towards infrared and ultraviolet in the extremes .	但他們更脆弱 , 可能在極端移動和紫外線之間的衝動 。
just to try and get an assessment of what our gene repertoire was , we assembled all the data including all of ours thus far from the expedition , which represents more than half of all the gene data on the planet and it totaled around 29 million genes .	試想一下 , 我們基因複製了所有基因資料 , 我們組組成的所有資料包括在地球上所有的基因資料包含了超過一半的基因資料 , 它代表超過超過2萬萬個基因資料 。
and we tried to put these into gene families to see what these discoveries are: are we just discovering new members of known families , or are we discovering new families ?	我們試著把這些基因放進基因家庭中 , 看看這些發現的:我們只是發現新的成員 , 或是我們發現新家庭的成員 ?
and it turns out we have about 50 , 000 major gene families , but every new sample we take in the environment adds in a linear fashion to these new families .	結果發現 , 我們有大約50000個基因家庭 , 但每一種新的樣本 。
so we're at the earliest stages of discovery about basic genes , components and life on this planet .	所以我們在最早期的發現 , 關於基本基因、元件和生命在這個星球上 。
when we look at the socalled evolutionary tree , we're up on the upper righthand corner with the animals .	當我們觀察到這麼冷靜的樹木時 , 我們在右邊的右邊 , 跟動物一樣 。
of those roughly 29 million genes , we only have around 24 , 000 in our genome .	在這些基因組中 , 我們只有超過29萬個基因組 , 我們只有超過24千萬個基因組 。
and if you take all animals together , we probably share less than 30 , 000 and probably maybe a dozen or more thousand different gene families .	如果你把所有動物一起在一起 , 我們可能分享不到30000個基因家庭 , 也許是數十個不同的基因家庭 。
i view that these genes are now not only the design components of evolution .	我現在認為這些基因不是唯一設計的元素 。
and we think in a genecentric view maybe going back to richard dawkins' ideas than in a genomecentric view , which are different constructs of these gene components .	我們認為在基因中心的觀點也許會回溯到花園的概念 , 比在基因組的觀點來看 , 不同建構的不同結構 。
synthetic dna , the ability to synthesize dna , has changed at sort of the same pace that dna sequencing has over the last decade or two , and is getting very rapid and very cheap .	合成dna、dna、dna、dna、dna序列的能力 , 改變dna序列的能力 。
our first thought about synthetic genomics came when we sequenced the second genome back in 1995 , and that from mycoplasma genitalium .	我們首先想到合合成基因組組組組成第二個基因組組組組成的第二個基因組 。
and we have really nice tshirts that say , you know , " i heart my genitalium . "	我們有很棒的椅子說: 「 我心臟病原 」
this is actually just a microorganism .	這其實只是個微生物學 。
but it has roughly 500 genes .	但它有大約500個基因 。
haemophilus had 1 , 800 genes .	哈佛博士有1800個基因 。
and we simply asked the question , if one species needs 800 , another 500 , is there a smaller set of genes that might comprise a minimal operating system ?	我們只是問這個問題 , 如果一個物種需要800 , 另一個500 , 另一個500 , 可能有比較小的基因運作系統 ?
so we started doing transposon mutagenesis .	所以我們開始做轉變突突變 。
transposons are just small pieces of dna that randomly insert in the genetic code .	相反的dna不僅僅是基因編碼的小部分 。
and if they insert in the middle of the gene , they disrupt its function .	如果他們在基因中間的中間 , 他們會破壞它 。
so we made a map of all the genes that could take transposon insertions and we called those " nonessential genes . "	所以我們做了一張所有基因的圖片 , 我們稱之為 「 無知基因 」 。
but it turns out the environment is very critical for this , and you can only define an essential or nonessential gene based on exactly what's in the environment .	但事實證明 , 環境非常重要的是 , 你只能定義一個必要或無意識基因基礎的基因基礎 。
we also tried to take a more directly intellectual approach with the genomes of 13 related organisms , and we tried to compare all of those , to see what they had in common .	我們也試著用更直接直接用13個體體體體內的基因組 , 我們試著把所有這些東西放在一起 , 看看它們有共同點 。
and we got these overlapping circles . and we found only 173 genes common to all 13 organisms .	我們得到了這些循環循環循環 , 我們發現只有173個基因共通點 。
the pool expanded a little bit if we ignored one intracellular parasite ; it expanded even more when we looked at core sets of genes of around 310 or so .	池塘擴展一下如果我們忽略了一塊垃圾寄生蟲的基因 , 它會擴展到310或所以當我們看著核心基因組的基因組 。
so we think that we can expand or contract genomes , depending on your point of view here , to maybe 300 to 400 genes from the minimal of 500 .	所以我們認為我們可以擴展或矛盾基因組 , 依賴你的觀點來看 , 也許300到4000個基因 。
the only way to prove these ideas was to construct an artificial chromosome with those genes in them , and we had to do this in a cassettebased fashion .	唯一方法證明這些想法是要建立一個人工染色體染色體染色體染色體
we found that synthesizing accurate dna in large pieces was extremely difficult .	我們發現 , 合成dna中的dna , 非常困難 。
ham smith and clyde hutchison , my colleagues on this , developed an exciting new method that allowed us to synthesize a 5 , 000base pair virus in only a twoweek period that was 100 percent accurate , in terms of its sequence and its biology .	哈姆斯mith和cartchion , 我的同事開發了一個新的方法 , 開發了一個新的方法 , 讓我們合作合作合作合作 , 只能將一百分之五千個巴基病毒 , 只剩兩年的生物學和生物學 。
it was a quite exciting experiment when we just took the synthetic piece of dna , injected it in the bacteria and all of a sudden , that dna started driving the production of the virus particles that turned around and then killed the bacteria .	這是很令人興奮的實驗當我們把dna拿出來的dna中 , 在細菌中 , dna開始開車 , dna開始開車 , dna開始開車 , dna開始打造細菌 。
this was not the first synthetic virus a polio virus had been made a year before but it was only one tenthousandth as active and it took three years to do .	這不是第一個合成的病毒病毒病毒 , 而是花了一年的時間 , 而是花了三年的時間 , 而是花了三年的時間 。
this is a cartoon of the structure of phi x 174 .	這是hix174年的結構 。
this is a case where the software now builds its own hardware , and that's the notions that we have with biology .	這是軟體現在的軟體 , 建造它自己的硬體 , 這不是我們與生物學的概念 。
people immediately jump to concerns about biological warfare , and i had recent testimony before a senate committee , and a special committee the u . s . government has set up to review this area .	人們會馬上跳到生物暖化之前 , 我最近有最近的試驗 , 我最近接觸到美國 , 一個特殊委員會 , 政府必須重新建議這個區域 。
and i think it's important to keep reality in mind , versus what happens with people's imaginations .	我認為這很重要的是要保持現實、平均想像力和人們想像力的想像力 。
basically , any virus that's been sequenced today that genome can be made .	基本上 , 任何病毒都被序列出來 。
and people immediately freak out about things about ebola or smallpox , but the dna from this organism is not infective .	人們馬上對伊波拉或小盒子 , 但這些生物從這個生物體中得到的dna , 但從這個生物體中得到的dna並不感染 。
so even if somebody made the smallpox genome , that dna itself would not cause infections .	所以即使有人做出小型的基因組 , dna本身不會造成感染 。
the real concern that security departments have is designer viruses .	真正的信念就是設計師病毒 。
and there's only two countries , the u . s . and the former soviet union , that had major efforts on trying to create biological warfare agents .	只有兩個國家 , 美國的總統 , 美國的總統 , 試圖創造生物暖化 , 試圖創造生物暖化的戰爭 。
if that research is truly discontinued , there should be very little activity on the knowhow to make designer viruses in the future .	如果這研究是非常失望的 , 應該有非常小的活動 , 應該在未來設計設計師的病毒 。
i think singlecell organisms are possible within two years .	我認為單一兩年內有機體 。
and possibly eukaryotic cells , those that we have , are possible within a decade .	可能是數十年來的氧化細胞 , 那些我們擁有的 , 可能在十年內 。
so we're now making several dozen different constructs , because we can vary the cassettes and the genes that go into this artificial chromosome .	我們現在正在製造數十個不同的建設 , 因為我們可以用貓咪和基因組的基因 。
the key is , how do you put all of the others ?	關鍵是 , 你要如何把所有其他人放在一起 ?
we start with these fragments , and then we have a homologous recombination system that reassembles those into a chromosome .	我們從這些碎片開始 , 然後我們有一個很大的回應系統 , 重新組合這些染色體 。
this is derived from an organism , deinococcus radiodurans , that can take three million rads of radiation and not be killed .	這是從生物體中取代生物 , 絕大多數的輻射 , 可以花三百萬個輻射 , 而不是被殺害 。
it reassembles its genome after this radiation burst in about 12 to 24 hours , after its chromosomes are literally blown apart .	在這個輻射後的基因組後 , 大約12到24小時後 , 染色體染色體是完全盲目的 。
this organism is ubiquitous on the planet , and exists perhaps now in outer space due to all our travel there .	這生物在地球上 , 存在於外太空 , 也許現在在外太空旅行中 , 可能在太空中所有的旅行 。
this is a glass beaker after about half a million rads of radiation .	這是一百萬個輻射後的玻璃比例 。
the glass started to burn and crack , while the microbes sitting in the bottom just got happier and happier .	玻璃開始燃燒和瘋狂 , 雖然微生物坐在底下 , 微生物坐在底下 , 更快樂和快樂 。
here's an actual picture of what happens: the top of this shows the genome after 1 . 7 million rads of radiation .	這是發生的事:這張圖顯示了1.7百萬個輻射的基因組 。
the chromosome is literally blown apart .	染色體是完全盲目的 。
and here's that same dna automatically reassembled 24 hours later .	這是同樣的dna自動複製了24小時後 。
it's truly stunning that these organisms can do that , and we probably have thousands , if not tens of thousands , of different species on this planet that are capable of doing that .	真的是這些生物可以做到這一點 , 而且我們可能有數千種不同的物種 , 如果我們沒有數千種不同的物種 。
after these genomes are synthesized , the first step is just transplanting them into a cell without a genome .	在這些基因組後後 , 第一步就是把它們移植到細胞裡 , 沒有基因組 。
so we think synthetic cells are going to have tremendous potential , not only for understanding the basis of biology but for hopefully environmental and society issues .	所以我們認為合成細胞將會有很大的潛力 , 不僅為了了解生物學和社會議題 。
for example , from the third organism we sequenced , methanococcus jannaschii it lives in boiling water temperatures ; its energy source is hydrogen and all its carbon comes from co2 it captures back from the environment .	舉例來說 , 從第三個機制中 , 甲烷佔據了水溫溫度 ; 它的能量 , 能源源源源自二氧化碳和所有碳從環境中捕捉到的二氧化碳 。
so we know lots of different pathways , thousands of different organisms now that live off of co2 , and can capture that back .	所以我們知道很多不同的路徑 , 數千種不同的生物 , 現在可以從二氧化碳中存活下來 。
so instead of using carbon from oil for synthetic processes , we have the chance of using carbon and capturing it back from the atmosphere , converting that into biopolymers or other products .	所以 , 不是用石油來合成碳和其他產品 。 我們有機會用碳和捕捉它從大氣中取出來 , 將它從大氣層或其他產品 。
we have one organism that lives off of carbon monoxide , and we use as a reducing power to split water to produce hydrogen and oxygen .	我們有一個有機機體 , 用碳分子來製造氫氣和氧氣 。
also , there's numerous pathways that can be engineered metabolizing methane .	同時 , 有很大的路徑 , 可以被工程化成甲烷 。
and dupont has a major program with statoil in norway to capture and convert the methane from the gas fields there into useful products .	而荷蘭有一大堆石油在挪威上 , 從氣體場到那裡 , 將甲烷從土壤中取得有用的產品 。
within a short while , i think there's going to be a new field called " combinatorial genomics , " because with these new synthesis capabilities , these vast gene array repertoires and the homologous recombination , we think we can design a robot to make maybe a million different chromosomes a day .	短短一段時間內 , 我認為有一種新的領域叫做 「 結合器 」 因為這些新合成基因組 」 因為有這些新合物可能性 , 我們認為我們可以設計機器人可以設計一個機器人 , 我們認為我們可以設計機器人可以製造一百萬種不同的染色體 , 我們認為我們可以設計機器人可以製造一百萬種不同的染色體 。
and therefore , as with all biology , you get selection through screening , whether you're screening for hydrogen production , or chemical production , or just viability .	因此 , 身為所有生物學 , 你可以透過螢幕來檢測氫化產品 , 不論你是否在螢幕上 , 或是化學產品 。
to understand the role of these genes is going to be well within reach .	為了了解這些基因的角色會很有效 。
we're trying to modify photosynthesis to produce hydrogen directly from sunlight .	我們試圖改造氫氣攝影機來製造氫氣直接從太陽光光光光光中產生氫氣
photosynthesis is modulated by oxygen , and we have an oxygeninsensitive hydrogenase that we think will totally change this process .	攝影機是由氧氣組成的 , 我們有一個氧氣感敏感的氫氣 , 我們認為不會改變這個過程 。
we're also combining cellulases , the enzymes that break down complex sugars into simple sugars and fermentation in the same cell for producing ethanol .	我們也將細胞組合成細胞組合 , 酵素將複雜的糖分解成簡單糖尿和脂肪相關 。
pharmaceutical production is already under way in major laboratories using microbes .	醫學產品已經在主要實驗室裡使用微生物生產微生物 。
the chemistry from compounds in the environment is orders of magnitude more complex than our best chemists can produce .	環境中的化學學家來自於環境中最複雜的化學物質 , 比我們最好的化學學家能生產 。
i think future engineered species could be the source of food , hopefully a source of energy , environmental remediation and perhaps replacing the petrochemical industry .	我認為未來工程師可以成為食物的源源頭 , 希望是環境的源頭 , 環境反覆性 , 也許再複製化學產業 。
let me just close with ethical and policy studies .	讓我和政策和政策研究 。
we delayed the start of our experiments in 1999 until we completed a yearandahalf bioethical review as to whether we should try and make an artificial species .	我們在1999年完成實驗 , 直到我們完成了實驗 , 直到我們是否應該嘗試創造一個人性的物種 。
every major religion participated in this .	在這個領域中 , 每個主要宗教參與者 。
it was actually a very strange study , because the various religious leaders were using their scriptures as law books , and they couldn't find anything in them prohibiting making life , so it must be ok . the only ultimate concerns were biological warfare aspects of this , but gave us the go ahead to start these experiments for the reasons we were doing them .	這是個非常奇怪的研究 , 因為許多宗教領袖使用他們的文章 , 他們不能在他們身上找到任何東西 , 所以他們不能在他們身上找到任何東西 , 所以它一定是生物暖化的 , 所以它一定是生物暖化的 , 但給予我們這個實驗 。
right now the sloan foundation has just funded a multiinstitutional study on this , to work out what the risk and benefits to society are , and the rules that scientific teams such as my own should be using in this area , and we're trying to set good examples as we go forward .	現在 , 西班牙基基金會已經資助了一個多種機構 , 找出風險和利益的規則 , 找出風險和社會的規則 , 就像我自己應該在這個區域中使用的規則 , 我們試著設定好的例子 。
these are complex issues .	這些都是複雜的問題 。
except for the threat of bioterrorism , they're very simple issues in terms of , can we design things to produce clean energy , perhaps revolutionizing what developing countries can do and provide through various simple processes .	除了生物恐怖主義的威脅 , 他們是非常簡單的問題 , 我們能設計東西來製造乾淨能源 , 也許革命發展出乾淨能源 , 也許革命發展出許多簡單的過程 。
psychologist philip zimbardo says happiness and success are rooted in a trait most of us disregard: the way we orient toward the past , present and future . he suggests we calibrate our outlook on time as a first step to improving our lives .	心理學家philipipzimbardo說幸福和成功有關 , 大部分美國人都被忽略了過去 , 未來 。 他建議了我們的人生方式:我們或未來 。 他建議我們的人生 。 他建議了我們的人生 。

life is temptation . it's all about yielding , resisting , yes , no , now , later , impulsive , reflective , present focus and future focus .	生命是跳舞 , 所有關於黃金、抗拒、抗拒、現在 , 等等 , 後來 , 反映、專注、專注、未來、專注、專注、未來、專注、未來 。
promised virtues fall prey to the passions of the moment .	承諾了視覺失敗的願景 。
of teenage girls who pledged sexual abstinence and virginity until marriage thank you george bush the majority , 60 percent , yielded to sexual temptations within one year .	青少年女孩被激發性虐待性虐待 , 直到婚姻 , 直到婚姻中 , 60%、60%、百分之六十 。
and most of them did so without using birth control .	大部分人都沒有用鳥類控制 。
so much for promises .	對於承諾 。
now lets tempt fouryearolds , giving them a treat .	現在讓我們暫停四歲的小孩 , 給他們一個治療 。
they can have one marshmallow now . but if they wait until the experimenter comes back , they can have two .	他們現在可以有一個馬鈴薯 , 但如果他們等到實驗者回來 , 他們就可以有兩個 。
of course it pays , if you like marshmallows , to wait .	當然 , 如果你喜歡馬鈴薯 , 等待你 。
what happens is twothirds of the kids give in to temptation .	接下來發生的是兩分之二的孩子 。
they cannot wait . the others , of course , wait .	他們不能等待 。 當然 , 等等 。
they resist the temptation . they delay the now for later .	他們現在抗拒 。 他們現在拒絕了 。
walter mischel , my colleague at stanford , went back 14 years later , to try to discover what was different about those kids .	華盛頓大學 , 我的同事在史丹佛大學 , 回到14年後 , 試圖發現這些孩子的不同 。
there were enormous differences between kids who resisted and kids who yielded , in many ways .	有很大的差異 , 那些被抗拒和孩子的孩子 , 在許多方面 , 以很多方面的差異 。
the kids who resisted scored 250 points higher on the sat .	那些抗拒了250個點 , 坐在土星上 。
that's enormous . that's like a whole set of different iq points .	這是很棒的 。 這是個不同的iq點 。
they didn't get in as much trouble . they were better students .	他們沒有太多麻煩了 , 他們更好的學生 。
they were selfconfident and determined . and the key for me today , the key for you , is , they were futurefocused rather than presentfocused .	他們很自信 , 今天對我來說 , 關鍵對你們來說 , 關鍵是 , 他們是未來的 。
so what is time perspective ? that's what i'm going to talk about today .	那麼 , 我今天要談什麼 ? 這就是我要談的 。
time perspective is the study of how individuals , all of us , divide the flow of your human experience into time zones or time categories .	時間觀點是個人經驗的研究 , 我們所有人體體體驗到時間zonezone或時間分配 。
and you do it automatically and nonconsciously .	然後你自動地做 , 沒有意識到 。
they vary between cultures , between nations , between individuals , between social classes , between education levels .	他們在文化之間之間之間之間之間 , 社會課程之間之間的差距 。
and the problem is that they can become biased , because you learn to overuse some of them and underuse the others .	問題是 , 他們可以變成偏見 , 因為你學會了一些人 , 把他們和其他人 。
what determines any decision you make ?	你是否做了什麼決定 ?
you make a decision on which you're going to base an action .	你決定要在哪裡做決定 。
for some people it's only about what is in the immediate situation , what other people are doing and what you're feeling .	對某些人來說 , 只有在立場的情況下 , 其他人正在做的事 , 你的感受 。
and those people , when they make their decisions in that format we're going to call them " presentoriented , " because their focus is what is now .	而那些人 , 當他們做出決策時 , 我們會稱他們為 「 現代 」 因為他們的焦點是現在的 。
for others , the present is irrelevant .	對其他人來說 , 現場是不可思議 。
it's always about " what is this situation like that i've experienced in the past ? "	一直在說: 「 我經歷過什麼樣子 ? 」
so that their decisions are based on past memories .	所以 , 他們的決策是根據過去記憶的 。
and we're going to call those people " pastoriented , " because they focus on what was .	我們要稱這些人為過去的人們 「 過去 」 因為他們專注在做什麼 。
for others it's not the past , it's not the present , it's only about the future .	對其他人來說 , 這不是過去 , 而是關於未來的 。
their focus is always about anticipated consequences .	他們的焦點是關於預期的結果 。
we're going to call them " futureoriented . " their focus is on what will be .	我們會稱他們為 「 未來 」 他們的焦點就是在什麼樣子上 。
so , time paradox , i want to argue , the paradox of time perspective , is something that influences every decision you make , you're totally unaware of .	所以 , 時間悖論 , 我想要爭論、時間的悖論 , 就是影響你每一個決策 , 你不會完全意識到你做出的影響 。
namely , the extent to which you have one of these biased time perspectives .	舉例來說 , 你有一份偏見的時間觀點 。
well there is actually six of them . there are two ways to be presentoriented .	其實有六種方法 , 有兩種方式是現代的 。
there is two ways to be pastoriented , two ways to be future .	過去有兩種方式 , 兩種方式是未來的 。
you can focus on pastpositive , or pastnegative .	你可以專注過去相反 , 或是過去負面的負面 。
you can be presenthedonistic , namely you focus on the joys of life , or presentfatalist it doesn't matter , your life is controlled .	你可以被描述生命的喜悅 , 稱之為生命的喜悅主義者的喜悅主義者並不重要 , 你的人生是控制的 。
you can be futureoriented , setting goals .	你可以是未來的 , 設定目標 。
or you can be transcendental future: namely , life begins after death .	或者 , 你可以被轉化為未來的未來:生命從死後開始 。
developing the mental flexibility to shift time perspectives fluidly depending on the demands of the situation , that's what you've got to learn to do .	開發出心理飛行時間的觀點 , 很有可能依賴情況下的需求 , 這就是你必須學習去做的事 。
so , very quickly , what is the optimal time profile ?	所以 , 很快地 , 什麼是最佳的時間 ?
high on pastpositive . moderately high on future .	過去相反 。 現代的高度高 。
and moderate on presenthedonism .	而現代主義在現代主義上 。
and always low on pastnegative and presentfatalism .	總是低於過去負面和現代主義 。
so the optimal temporal mix is what you get from the past pastpositive gives you roots . you connect your family , identity and your self .	所以 , 最樂觀的混合是你從過去的過去 , 讓你的家人 , 你連結你的家人 , 身份和你的自我連結 。
what you get from the future is wings to soar to new destinations , new challenges .	從未來開始 , 你從未來到新的辯論、新的挑戰 。
what you get from the present hedonism is the energy , the energy to explore yourself , places , people , sensuality .	你從現代主義中得到的能量 , 能量來探索自己、地方、人、人、人們、敏感 。
any time perspective in excess has more negatives than positives .	每次觀點比正面的觀點比正面 。
what do futures sacrifice for success ?	未來的成功呢 ?
they sacrifice family time . they sacrifice friend time .	他們的犧牲家庭時間 , 他們犧牲朋友 。
they sacrifice fun time . they sacrifice personal indulgence .	他們的犧牲時間 , 他們犧牲了個人成人 。
they sacrifice hobbies . and they sacrifice sleep . so it affects their health .	他們犧牲了飯店 , 他們的犧牲睡眠 。 所以它影響他們的健康 。
and they live for work , achievement and control .	他們為工作、成就和控制 。
i'm sure that resonates with some of the tedsters .	我相信 , 有一些tedter的反應 。
and it resonated for me . i grew up as a poor kid in the south bronx ghetto , a sicilian family everyone lived in the past and present .	對我來說 , 我長大了 , 我長大 , 身為南布朗克斯的小孩子 , 一位醫師家人住在過去和現在 。
i'm here as a futureoriented person who went over the top , who did all these sacrifices because teachers intervened , and made me future oriented .	我在這裡來這裡是一位未來的奧運人 , 他們做了所有犧牲的犧牲 , 因為老師介紹師介紹了 , 讓我未來或有智慧 。
told me don't eat that marshmallow , because if you wait you're going to get two of them , until i learned to balance out .	對我來說 , 不要吃馬鈴薯 , 因為如果你等等等待你 , 直到我學到平衡 。
i've added presenthedonism , i've added a focus on the pastpositive , so , at 76 years old , i am more energetic than ever , more productive , and i'm happier than i have ever been .	我已經加入了過去主義 , 我把焦點放在過去的過去76歲 , 所以 , 在過去76歲的時候 , 我比以前更有生產力 , 我比以前更快樂 。
i just want to say that we are applying this to many world problems: changing the dropout rates of school kids , combating addictions , enhancing teen health , curing vets' ptsd with time metaphors getting miracle cures promoting sustainability and conservation , reducing physical rehabilitation where there is a 50percent drop out rate , altering appeals to suicidal terrorists , and modifying family conflicts as timezone clashes .	我只想說 , 我們正在應用很多問題:改變學校的戲劇率 , 讓青少年的飲食率 , 讓疫苗變得很奇怪 , 讓疫苗變得很奇怪 , 將免疫疾病轉換為永續發展的永續性和保育 , 減少50年代的身體 , 減少了五十五十個家庭抗生素 。
so i want to end by saying: many of life's puzzles can be solved by understanding your time perspective and that of others .	所以我想要結束說:許多生命的謎題可以被理解 , 你的觀點 , 以及其他人的觀點 。
and the idea is so simple , so obvious , but i think the consequences are really profound .	這個想法很簡單 , 但我認為結果是很明顯的 , 但我認為結果是非常深刻的 。

now , the saturn system is a rich planetary system .	現在 , 土星系統是一個豐富的星系 。

now , two of the 47 moons that saturn has are standouts .	現在 , 第四7月47月47月47日 。
and those are titan and enceladus . titan is saturn's largest moon , and , until cassini had arrived there , was the largest single expanse of unexplored terrain that we had remaining in our solar system .	而這些不是西班牙和伊斯蘭人是土星最大的月球 , 直到柬埔寨最大的月球 , 直到柬埔寨 , 直到我們的太陽系中 , 最大型的單位 。
and it is a body that has long intrigued people who've watched the planets .	這是個身體 , 一個身體已經長久了 。
it has a very large , thick atmosphere , and in fact , its surface environment was believed to be more like the environment we have here on the earth , or at least had in the past , than any other body in the solar system .	事實上 , 它有一個非常大的厚度 , 事實上 , 它表面環境的表面 , 表面環境的環境 , 或至少在過去 , 在太陽系中 , 至少在太陽系中任何其他身體中都有 。
its atmosphere is largely molecular nitrogen , like you are breathing here in this room , except that its atmosphere is suffused with simple organic materials like methane and propane and ethane .	它的大氣層很大的分子 , 就像你在這個房間裡呼吸 , 例如你正在呼吸的簡單分子 , 例如甲烷和財富一樣 。
and these molecules high up in the atmosphere of titan get broken down , and their products join together to make haze particles .	這些分子在大氣中的大氣層高高高高高峰 , 他們的產品會加入粒子 。
this haze is ubiquitous . it's completely global and enveloping titan .	這棲息是全球和土耳其 , 完全是全球和鼓舞 。
and that's why you cannot see down to the surface with our eyes in the visible region of the spectrum .	這就是為什麼你看不到的表面 。
but these haze particles , it was surmised , before we got there with cassini , over billions and billions of years , gently drifted down to the surface and coated the surface in a thick organic sludge .	但這些討厭粒子 , 在我們和一些洞穴之前 , 在我們和洞穴中 , 有超過十億年來 , 顯然地把表放在厚厚厚厚厚的生物學 。
so like the equivalent , the titan equivalent , of tar , or oil , or what we didn't know what .	就像蚊子一樣 , 西班牙牙 , 或是石油、石油、石油、油、油、油、油、我們不知道什麼 。
but this is what we suspected . and these molecules , especially methane and ethane , can be liquids at the surface temperatures of titan .	但這是我們猜測的 。 這些分子 , 特別是甲烷和乙醇 , 特別是甲烷和乙醇 , 可以在西班牙的溫度 。
and so it turns out that methane is to titan what water is to the earth .	結果發現 , 甲烷是地球的 。
it's a condensable in the atmosphere , and so recognizing this circumstance brought to the fore a whole world of bizarre possibilities . you can have methane clouds , ok , and above those clouds , you have this hundreds of kilometers of haze , which prevent any sunlight from getting to the surface .	這是大氣層的大氣層 , 所以認知這個圓圈帶到整個世界各地的可能性 , 你可以遇到許多奇怪的可能性 。 你可以遇到阿富汗雲朵 , 好吧 , 你有數百公里的雲朵 , 你有了數百公里的陽光 。
the temperature at the surface is some 350 degrees below zero fahrenheit .	表面的溫度是有350度的零度 。
but despite that cold , you could have rain falling down on the surface of titan .	但儘管如此 , 你可能有雨水的表面 。
and doing on titan what rain does on the earth: it carves gullies ; it forms rivers and cataracts ; it can create canyons ; it can pool in large basins and craters .	地球上的雨林做的事:它會造成河流 , 它形成河流 , 形成河流、貓咪、貓咪、貓咪 , 可以在大細菌和螃蟹 。
it can wash the sludge off high mountain peaks and hills , down into the lowlands . so stop and think for a minute .	它可以引起高山山頂高山的山頂 , 到低地下 , 停下來 , 停下來 , 停下來思考一下 。
try to imagine what the surface of titan might look like .	試著想像一下英國表面的表面 。
it's dark . high noon on titan is as dark as deep earth twilight on the earth .	它是黑暗的 , 高隆在地球上最深的地球上 。

we have instruments on cassini which can see down to the surface through this atmosphere , and my camera system is one of them .	我們在柬埔寨的基礎設施 , 可以看到大氣層的表面 , 我的攝影機是其中之一 。

whenever you see anything linear on a planet , it means there's been a fracture , like a fault .	當你在地球上看到任何東西時 , 它意味著有架構 , 就像一個公平 。

but we couldn't make sense of our images , until , six months after we got into orbit , an event occurred that many have regarded as the highlight of cassini's investigation of titan .	但我們無法理解我們的影像 , 直到 , 直到我們進入軌道上 , 大約六個月後 , 甚至發生在西班牙的調查 。
and that was the deployment of the huygens probe , the europeanbuilt huygens probe that cassini had carried for seven years across the solar system . we deployed it to the atmosphere of titan , it took two and a half hours to descend , and it landed on the surface .	這就是飢餓的探測器 , 歐洲布爾•布萊恩•布爾•布萊恩•布萊恩•布萊恩 , 我們將它帶到太陽系大氣層的大氣層 , 花了兩半小時 , 花了兩半小時的時間 , 它在表面上 。

that's as bizarre as finding that the antarctic on the earth is hotter than the tropics .	這是地球上最奇怪的發現 , 比川普的熱情比川普的熱情 。
and then , when we took additional pictures , we discovered that from these fractures are issuing jets of fine , icy particles extending hundreds of miles into space .	接著 , 當我們把這些框架放在這些框架中 , 我們發現從這些框架中發現 , 粒子在太空中 , 粒子在太空中 。
and when we colorcode this image , to bring out the faint light levels , we see that these jets feed a plume that , in fact , we see , in other images , goes thousands of miles into the space above enceladus .	當我們編碼這張圖片時 , 我們看到這些噴射光層 , 事實上 , 我們看到這些噴射器 , 事實上 , 在其他影像中 , 在其他影像中看到的 , 經過數千英里的英里 。

and we have arrived at the conclusion that these jets may be erupting from pockets of liquid water under the surface of enceladus .	我們在這個結論中 , 這些猶太人可能是從液體表面上抽出來的水面上 。

in other words , we have possibly stumbled upon the holy grail of modern day planetary exploration , or in other words , an environment that is potentially suitable for living organisms .	換句話說 , 我們有可能很穩定的地球探索 , 或換句話說 , 可能是永續生物探索生物體的環境 。
and i don't think i need to tell you that the discovery of life elsewhere in our solar system , whether it be on enceladus or elsewhere , would have enormous cultural and scientific implications .	我不認為我需要告訴各位 , 在太陽系中其他地方 , 不論是在奴隸或其他地方 , 不論是在奴隸或其他地方 , 會有很大的文化和科學進步 。
because if we could demonstrate that genesis had occurred not once , but twice , independently , in our solar system , then that means , by inference , it has occurred a staggering number of times throughout the universe and its 13 . 7 billion year history .	因為如果我們可以偵測到基因噪音中沒有一次 , 但在我們的太陽系中 , 獨立地 , 在我們的太陽系中 , 這意味著 , 在我們的太陽系中 , 這意味著 , 藉由影響宇宙和13.7億7億年歷史 。
right now , earth is the only planet still that we know is teeming with life .	現在 , 地球是唯一的行星仍然存在著生命 。
it is precious , it is unique , it is still , so far , the only home we've ever known .	它很珍貴 , 它仍然是獨特的 , 所以 , 我們唯一知道的 。
and if any of you were alert and coherent during the 1960s and we'd forgive you , if you weren't , ok you would remember this very famous picture taken by the apollo 8 astronauts in 1968 .	如果你們在1960年代時 , 我們就會忘記你 , 如果你不認知你 , 如果你不 , 你就會記得這個非常有名的照片 , 由阿波波羅8年太空人拍攝的照片 。
it was the first time that earth was imaged from space , and it had an enormous impact on our sense of place in the universe , and our sense of responsibility for the protection of our own planet .	這是地球上第一次 , 地球上的影像 , 它有很大的影響力 , 而我們對地球的責任 。 我們的責任 。
well , we on cassini have taken an equivalent first , a picture that no human eye has ever seen before .	嗯 , 我們在柬埔寨拍攝的第一張照片 , 沒有人看過 。
it is a total eclipse of the sun , seen from the other side of saturn .	這是太陽的另一邊 , 從土星的另一端 , 從土星的另一端 。
and in this impossibly beautiful picture , you see the main rings backlit by the sun , you see the refracted image of the sun and you see this ring created , in fact , by the exhalations of enceladus .	在這個不可能的照片中 , 你看到了太陽系的主要節奏 , 你看到這張圖片的圖像 , 事實上 , 你看到這個節奏的圖像 。
but as if that weren't brilliant enough , we can spot , in this beautiful image , sight of our own planet , cradled in the arms of saturn's rings .	但如果那不是太棒了 , 我們可以把這個漂亮的圖像 , 在這個美麗的圖像 , 瘋狂的角度 , 瘋狂的角度 。
now , there is something deeply moving about seeing ourselves from afar , and capturing the sight of our little , blueocean planet in the skies of other worlds .	現在 , 有一件很深刻地移動我們小小、捕捉我們自己的小小、藍色的星球 。
and that , and the perspective of ourselves that we gain from that , may be , in the end , the finest reward that we earn from this journey of discovery that started half a century ago .	此外 , 我們自己從那一趟旅程的觀點來看 , 最後 , 最好的獎勵 , 在半世紀前 , 我們從這個旅程開始 。
as of 2005 , only 15 percent of the world was mapped . this slows the delivery of aid after a disaster and hides the economic potential of unused lands and unknown roads . in this short talk , google's lalitesh katragadda demos map maker , a group mapmaking tool that people around the globe are using to map their world .	2005年 , 世界上只有15% , 只有15%的援助和隱藏的經濟潛力 , 隱藏在這個短演講後 , google的經濟潛力 , 在這個短演講中 , google是拉丁美洲的地圖 。
collaboration , design , map , technology	合作、設計、地圖、圖、地圖、技術、技術、技術 。
lalitesh katragadda: making maps to fight disaster , build economies	晚餐katragada:讓地圖來對抗災難 , 建立經濟體 。
in 2008 , cyclone nargis devastated myanmar .	2008年 , 循環了我的耳朵 。
millions of people were in severe need of help .	數百萬人在秘密需要幫助 。
the u . n . wanted to rush people and supplies to the area .	美國 , 想要打破人們和供應到區域 。
but there were no maps , no maps of roads , no maps showing hospitals , no way for help to reach the cyclone victims .	但沒有地圖 , 沒有地圖 , 沒有地圖顯示醫院的地圖 , 沒有幫助到達循環 。
when we look at a map of los angeles or london , it is hard to believe that as of 2005 , only 15 percent of the world was mapped to a geocodable level of detail .	當我們看著洛杉磯或倫敦的地圖 , 很難相信2005年 , 世界上只有15% , 只有15%的細節 。
the u . n . ran headfirst into a problem that the majority of the world's populous faces: not having detailed maps .	聯合國 , 伊朗總統在世界上大部分的臉孔:沒有細節的地圖:沒有細節地圖 。
but help was coming .	但幫助是來了 。
at google , 40 volunteers used a new software to map 120 , 000 kilometers of roads , 3 , 000 hospitals , logistics and relief points .	在google , 40個志工使用一個新的軟體 , 40個醫院 , 000公里的醫院 , 有3 , 000公里、信仰、邏輯、信仰、邏輯和宗教信仰 。
and it took them four days .	它花了四天的時間 。
the new software they used ? google mapmaker .	新軟體會使用嗎 ? googlemakerer 。
google mapmaker is a technology that empowers each of us to map what we know locally .	googlemaker是一項科技 , 我們每個人都能繪製我們所知的科技 。
people have used this software to map everything from roads to rivers , from schools to local businesses , and video stores to the corner store .	人們用這種軟體來繪製所有東西 , 從學校到當地企業、影片、影片、影片、影片、影片、影片、影片等等 。
nobel prize nominee hernando de soto recognized that the key to economic liftoff for most developing countries is to tap the vast amounts of uncapitalized land .	諾貝爾獎獎獎賞她兒子的關鍵是 , 大部分開發中國家的關鍵 , 就是要為大部分開發中國家的資產 。
for example , a trillion dollars of real estate remains uncapitalized in india alone .	舉例來說 , 一兆美元在印度的印度 。
in the last year alone , thousands of users in 170 countries have mapped millions of pieces of information , and created a map of a level of detail never thought viable .	在過去一年 , 數以千計的使用者在170個國家裡 , 創造了數百萬件細節的地圖 , 創造了一層細節 。
and this was made possible by the power of passionate users everywhere .	這就是熱情使用者的力量 。
let's look at some of the maps being created by users right now .	讓我們看看一些地圖是由使用者所創造的 。
so , as we speak , people are mapping the world in these 170 countries .	所以 , 當我們說話 , 人們在這個1770個國家 。
you can see bridget in africa who just mapped a road in senegal .	你可以看到在非洲的橋樑中橋樑的橋樑 。
and , closer to home , chalua , an n . g . road in bangalore .	更接近回家 , 查爾 , 一個n.g.road在巴黎的路上 。
this is the result of computational geometry , gesture recognition , and machine learning .	這是計算計算機的結果結果 , 高度認知 , 以及機器學習 。
this is a victory of thousands of users , in hundreds of cities , one user , one edit at a time .	這是數千個使用者 , 在數百個城市裡 , 其中一個使用者 , 其中一個使用者 。
this is an invitation to the 70 percent of our unmapped planet .	這是一個邀請地球70%的未被應用在地球上 。
welcome to the new world .	歡迎到新世界 。
in 2003 , the palestinian village of budrus mounted a 10monthlong nonviolent protest to stop a barrier being built across their olive groves . did you hear about it ? didn't think so . brazilian filmmaker julia bacha asks why we only pay attention to violence in the israelpalestine conflict and not to the nonviolent leaders who may one day bring peace .	2003年 , 巴勒斯坦的村落 , 巴勒斯坦的村落 , 巴勒斯坦的抗議 , 你聽見了嗎 ? 不認為 , 巴西的電影會問:我們為什麼只注意到 , 我們只注意到 , 巴西電影中 , 我們只注意到 , 沒有人注意到暴力和平 。
arts , communication , compassion , entertainment , film , peace , violence , war	藝術、溝通、同情、娛樂、電影、電影、暴力、暴力、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、戰爭、
julia bacha: pay attention to nonviolence	朱利亞•巴克:注意到非暴力暴力 。
for the last 8 years , i have dedicated my life to documenting the work of israelis and palestinians who are trying to end the conflict using peaceful means .	過去8年來 , 我已經把我的人生記錄下來 , 就是伊拉爾和巴勒斯坦人在試圖結束衝突使用和平靜的意義 。
when i travel with my work across europe and the united states , one question always comes up: where is the palestinian gandhi ?	當我和美國各地的工作時 , 其中一個問題總是出現:哪裡是巴勒斯坦甘地 ?
why aren't palestinians using nonviolent resistance ?	為什麼不是巴勒斯坦使用非暴力抗拒 ?
the challenge i face when i hear this question is that often i have just returned from the middle east where i spent my time filming dozens of palestinians who are using nonviolence to defend their lands and water resources from israeli soldiers and settlers .	當我聽到這個問題時 , 我聽到這個問題時 , 我剛剛從中東東東部的挑戰是 , 我花了幾十個巴勒斯坦人使用非暴力來保護他們的土地和水資源資源來自伊拉利利亞和設立者 。
these leaders are trying to forge a massive national nonviolent movement to end the occupation and build peace in the region .	這些領導者正在試圖忘記一個巨大的國家非暴力運動 , 並建立和平靜的活動 。
yet , most of you have probably never heard about them .	然而 , 大部分人可能從未聽過他們 。
this divide between what's happening on the ground and perceptions abroad is one of the key reasons why we don't have yet a palestinian peaceful resistance movement that has been successful .	這距離在地面和感知之間的差別之一就是為什麼我們還沒有巴勒斯坦和平的抗議運動之一之一 。
so i'm here today to talk about the power of attention , the power of your attention , and the emergence and development of nonviolent movements in the west bank , gaza and elsewhere but today , my case study is going to be palestine .	所以我今天來這裡談注意力的力量力量 , 以及你的注意力 , 以及非暴力運動的力量 , 在西方銀行、gaza、gaza和其他地方 , 我的研究將會是巴勒斯坦的 。
i believe that what's mostly missing for nonviolence to grow is not for palestinians to start adopting nonviolence , but for us to start paying attention to those who already are .	我相信 , 大部分都沒暴力 , 要開始成長並不是為了巴勒斯坦的非暴力 , 而是為了我們開始注意到那些已經開始注意到這些人 。
allow me to illustrate this point by taking you to this village called budrus .	讓我介紹一下這個村落叫做budrudrudrudrudrudrus 。
about seven years ago , they faced extinction , because israel announced it would build a separation barrier , and part of this barrier would be built on top of the village .	大約七年前 , 他們面面臨滅絕 , 因為伊拉爾宣佈它會建立一個分離的障礙 , 而這條條障礙會在村莊的頂端 。
they would lose 40 percent of their land and be surrounded , so they would lose free access to the rest of the west bank .	他們會失去40%的土地 , 所以他們會失去40% , 所以他們會失去西方銀行 。
through inspired local leadership , they launched a peaceful resistance campaign to stop that from happening .	透過啟發當地領導力 , 他們發了一個和平靜的活動 , 他們發了一個和平靜的活動 , 停止發生 。
let me show you some brief clips , so you have a sense for what that actually looked like on the ground .	讓我給各位看一些令人驚訝的影片 , 所以你有感興趣 。

here in budrus , we realized the wall would steal our land .	在budrudrudrudrudrus , 我們意識到牆壁 。

woman: we saw the men trying to push the soldiers , but none of them could do that .	女士:我們看到男人試圖把士兵打開 , 但沒有人能這麼做 。
but i think the girls could do it .	但我認為女孩可以做到 。
fatah party member: we must empty our minds of traditional thinking .	假如黨派:我們必須擁抱傳統思想 。

fatah , hamas and the popular front !	假如 , 哈馬和受歡迎 。

but there were others around me who weren't even cowering .	但在我周圍的其他人甚至沒有在牛肉身上 。
israeli soldier: a nonviolent protest is not going to stop the [unclear] .	伊拉利斯:一個非暴力抗議的抗議不會阻止 「 非暴力 」 。

julia bacha: when i first heard about the story of budrus , i was surprised that the international media had failed to cover the extraordinary set of events that happened seven years ago , in 2003 .	朱利亞•巴克:當我第一次聽到布魯德媒體的故事時 , 我很驚訝的是國際媒體失敗的事件 , 七年前 , 2003年 , 在2003年之前 ,
what was even more surprising was the fact that budrus was successful .	更令人驚訝的是 , 布魯德的事實是成功的 。
the residents , after 10 months of peaceful resistance , convinced the israeli government to move the route of the barrier off their lands and to the green line , which is the internationally recognized boundary between israel and the palestinian territories .	在10個月後 , 和平靜的抗拒後 , 相信伊拉斯蘭政府搬到他們的土地和綠線之間 , 以色列的路線和綠線之間 , 這是國際的國際關係 , 這是巴爾和巴勒斯坦人之間的關係 。
the resistance in budrus has since spread to villages across the west bank and to palestinian neighborhoods in jerusalem .	布魯德的抗拒從西方移到西方的鄰居和巴勒斯坦的鄰居 。
yet the media remains mostly silent on these stories .	然而媒體仍然在這些故事上 ,
this silence carries profound consequences for the likelihood that nonviolence can grow , or even survive , in palestine .	這種寂靜的卡路里很深刻的後果 , 沒有暴力可以成長 , 或者甚至存活下來 , 在巴勒斯林中 , 甚至存活下來 。
violent resistance and nonviolent resistance share one very important thing in common ; they are both a form of theater seeking an audience to their cause .	暴力抗拒和非暴力抗拒分享一個很重要的事情 , 他們兩者都是個非常重要的事 ; 他們兩種觀眾的形式 。
if violent actors are the only ones constantly getting frontpage covers and attracting international attention to the palestinian issue , it becomes very hard for nonviolent leaders to make the case to their communities that civil disobedience is a viable option in addressing their plight .	如果暴力的演員是唯一的 , 只有一個持續的勇氣和吸引國際議題 , 它變得非常難以置信的議題 , 它變得非常困難 , 讓非暴力領導者能夠讓他們的社區變得更難以置信 。
the power of attention is probably going to come as no surprise to the parents in the room .	注意力的力量可能是沒有驚訝的父母 。
the surest way to make your child throw increasingly louder tantrums is by giving him attention the first time he throws a fit .	確保你的孩子扔進嬰兒時 , 最早的抗藥性是透過他注意到 , 他第一次把他的注意力丟掉 。
the tantrum will become what childhood psychologists call a functional behavior , since the child has learned that he can get parental attention out of it .	螞蟻會成為童年心理學家稱之為 「 功能行為行為行為 」 的孩子發現 , 他可以得到父母的注意力 。
parents can incentivize or disincentivize behavior simply by giving or withdrawing attention to their children .	父母可以激勵或分散行為 , 只是透過給孩子的注意力 , 只透過他們的孩子 。
but that's true for adults too .	但這也是如此 。
in fact , the behavior of entire communities and countries can be influenced , depending on where the international community chooses to focus its attention .	事實上 , 整個社區和國家的行為行為可以影響它的影響 , 依賴國際社區選擇專注於注意力 。
i believe that at the core of ending the conflict in the middle east and bringing peace is for us to transform nonviolence into a functional behavior by giving a lot more attention to the nonviolent leaders on the ground today .	我相信 , 在中東的核心衝突 , 帶給我們非暴力的核心是為了改變非暴力領導人的行為 。
in the course of taking my film to villages in the west bank , in gaza and in east jerusalem , i have seen the impact that even one documentary film can have in influencing the transformation .	在西方銀行的過程中 , 在加薩和東京 , 在加薩和東京的電影中 , 我看到的影響 , 即使有一個文件可以影響改變改變改變改變 。
in a village called wallajeh , which sits very close to jerusalem , the community was facing a very similar plight to budrus .	在一個村莊中 , 這個村落非常近猶太人 , 社區正在面對猶太人 , 社區正在面對虐待 。
they were going to be surrounded , lose a lot of their lands and not have freedom of access , either to the west bank or jerusalem .	他們會被繁殖 , 失去許多土地 , 失去許多土地 , 不需要取得、或猶太人 。
they had been using nonviolence for about two years but had grown disenchanted since nobody was paying attention .	他們一直在使用非暴力的兩年 , 但從沒有人注意力 , 因為沒有人在乎注意力 。
so we organized a screening .	所以我們組織化了一個螢幕 。
a week later , they held the most wellattended and disciplined demonstration to date .	一週後 , 他們告訴了最好的展示和歧視的描述 。
the organizers say that the villagers , upon seeing the story of budrus documented in a film , felt that there were indeed people following what they were doing , that people cared .	組織說 , 村民們說 , 去看看佛羅德的故事的故事的故事 , 感覺到 , 人們在追蹤他們所做的 , 人們追蹤他們在做什麼 , 人們追蹤他們所做的 。
so they kept on going .	所以他們繼續下去 。
on the israeli side , there is a new peace movement called solidariot , which means solidarity in hebrew .	在伊拉利亞 , 有一種新的和平的運動運動 , 這意味著很令人驚訝的運動 。
the leaders of this movement have been using budrus as one of their primary recruiting tools .	這項運動的領導者一直在使用虐待工具之一 。
they report that israelis who had never been active before , upon seeing the film , understand the power of nonviolence and start joining their activities .	他們報告是raelisisisis從來沒有活躍 , 了解非暴力的力量 , 開始加入他們的活動 。
the examples of wallajeh and the solidariot movement show that even a smallbudget independent film can play a role in transforming nonviolence into a functional behavior .	牆壁和索利亞的例子顯示 , 即使在獨立電影中 , 甚至是獨立的小預算 , 改變非暴力行為的行為 。
now imagine the power that big media players could have if they started covering the weekly nonviolent demonstrations happening in villages like bil'in , ni'lin , wallajeh , in jerusalem neighborhoods like sheikh jarrah and silwan the nonviolent leaders would become more visible , valued and effective in their work .	想像一下大媒體的力量 , 如果他們開始在村莊裡沒有暴力的示範 , 像巴勒斯坦 , 像巴勒斯坦 , 在猶太人 , 在耶魯的鄰居 , 在猶太人 , 沒有暴力 , 沒有暴力的領導人會變得更有效 。
i believe that the most important thing is to understand that if we don't pay attention to these efforts , they are invisible , and it's as if they never happened .	我相信最重要的事情是要了解 , 如果我們不注意到這些努力 , 它們是不可能發生的 , 而如果他們從未發生過 。
but i have seen first hand that if we do , they will multiply .	但我看到第一張手 , 如果我們這麼做 , 他們會多重 。
if they multiply , their influence will grow in the overall israelipalestinian conflict .	如果他們多久 , 他們的影響會在巴勒斯坦衝突的衝突 。
and theirs is the kind of influence that can finally unblock the situation .	他們的影響是無法阻止情況 。
these leaders have proven that nonviolence works in places like budrus .	這些領導者已經證明了非暴力工作 , 比如布魯德魯斯工作 。
let's give them attention so they can prove it works everywhere .	讓我們注意一下 , 可以證明它可以在任何地方 。
simon sinek has a simple but powerful model for inspirational leadership all starting with a golden circle and the question " why ? " his examples include apple , martin luther king , and the wright brothers . . .	西蒙有很簡單但強大的啟發 , 為何呢 ? 為什麼 ? 蘋果蘋果蘋果蘋果蘋果、馬丁•金恩•金恩博士 。
bullseye , business , entrepreneur , leadership , sales , selling , success	bully、企業家、企業家、企業家、企業、銷售、銷售、成功、成功、成功、成功、成功、成功、成功、成功、成功、成功、成功、成功、成功、成功、商業、商業、企業家
simon sinek: how great leaders inspire action	西蒙汀:多麼偉大的領導人 。
how do you explain when things don't go as we assume ?	你怎麼解釋當事情不像我們假設假設什麼 ?
or better , how do you explain when others are able to achieve things that seem to defy all of the assumptions ?	或者更好 , 你要如何解釋 , 當其他人能夠達到所有假設的假設 ?
for example: why is apple so innovative ?	舉例來說:為什麼蘋果兒子蘋果 ?
year after year , after year , after year , they're more innovative than all their competition .	一年後 , 一年後 , 他們比所有的競爭都更創新 。
and yet , they're just a computer company .	然而 , 他們只是一個電腦公司公司 。
they're just like everyone else .	他們就像其他人一樣 。
they have the same access to the same talent , the same agencies , the same consultants , the same media .	他們擁有同樣的能力 , 同樣的基因組 , 同樣的基因組 , 相同的標準 , 同樣的媒體 。
then why is it that they seem to have something different ?	為什麼他們似乎有不同 ?
why is it that martin luther king led the civil rights movement ?	為什麼火星權運動會導致民權運動 ?
he wasn't the only man who suffered in a precivil rights america , and he certainly wasn't the only great orator of the day .	他不是唯一受苦的男人 , 他肯定不是唯一偉大的人 , 他肯定不是唯一偉大的或一天 。
and why is it that the wright brothers were able to figure out controlled , powered man flight when there were certainly other teams who were better qualified , better funded . . .	為什麼這是最糟糕的兄弟能夠找出控制控制、強迫的男士飛行時 , 當有一些更好的隊伍 , 更好玩 。
and they didn't achieve powered man flight , and the wright brothers beat them to it .	他們沒有成就了男人飛行 , 兄弟們會把他們送到它 。
there's something else at play here .	這裡還有其他東西 。
about three and a half years ago i made a discovery .	大約三到半年前 , 我做了一個發現 。
and this discovery profoundly changed my view on how i thought the world worked , and it even profoundly changed the way in which i operate in it .	這發現了我對世界運作的觀點改變了我的觀點 , 它甚至很深刻改變了我如何運作的方式 。
as it turns out , there's a pattern .	結果發現 , 有一個模式 。
as it turns out , all the great and inspiring leaders and organizations in the world whether it's apple or martin luther king or the wright brothers they all think , act and communicate the exact same way .	結果發現 , 所有的偉大、鼓舞領導人和組織 , 不論是蘋果或馬丁•金恩 , 他們都認為 , 行為和兄弟們溝通 。
and it's the complete opposite to everyone else .	這是完全相反的完全相反 。
all i did was codify it , and it's probably the world's simplest idea .	我所做的都是編碼 , 可能是世界上最簡單的想法 。
i call it the golden circle .	我稱它為黃金圓圈 。
why ? how ? what ?	為什麼 ?
this little idea explains why some organizations and some leaders are able to inspire where others aren't .	這個小想法解釋為什麼有些組織和一些領導人都無法啟發 。
let me define the terms really quickly .	讓我解釋一下這個詞真的很快 。
every single person , every single organization on the planet knows what they do , 100 percent .	每個人 , 每個組織都知道他們做什麼 , 每一位組織都有100% 。
some know how they do it , whether you call it your differentiated value proposition or your proprietary process or your usp .	有些人知道他們怎麼做 , 不論你稱它為你的不同的價值觀 , 或是你的財產過程 。
but very , very few people or organizations know why they do what they do .	但非常非常少的人或組織知道他們怎麼做 。
and by " why " i don't mean " to make a profit . "	順便說: 「 我為何 」 。
that's a result . it's always a result .	這是結果 。 它總是是個結果 。
by " why , " i mean: what's your purpose ?	順便說: 「 為什麼 , 你的目的 ? 」
what's your cause ? what's your belief ?	你的原因是什麼 ? 你的信念 ?
why does your organization exist ?	為什麼你的組織存在 ?
why do you get out of bed in the morning ?	為什麼你從早上拿出來 ?
and why should anyone care ?	為什麼有人會照顧 ?
well , as a result , the way we think , the way we act , the way we communicate is from the outside in .	結果 , 我們認為 , 我們行動的方式是從外面溝通的方式溝通方式溝通的方式 。
it's obvious . we go from the clearest thing to the fuzziest thing .	很顯然 , 我們從最清楚的事情到難民 。
but the inspired leaders and the inspired organizations regardless of their size , regardless of their industry all think , act and communicate from the inside out .	但激勵領導者和鼓勵組織 , 不論他們的尺寸 , 除非他們的產業都認為 , 行動和內部的產業 。
let me give you an example .	讓我舉個例子 。
i use apple because they're easy to understand and everybody gets it .	我用蘋果 , 因為他們很容易了解 , 每個人都得到它 。
if apple were like everyone else , a marketing message from them might sound like this: " we make great computers .	如果蘋果就像其他人一樣 , 一個市場傳遞訊息 , 聽起來像這樣: 「 我們製造偉大的電腦 」 。
they're beautifully designed , simple to use and user friendly .	他們很漂亮的設計 , 簡單使用和使用者友善的方式 。
want to buy one ? " " meh . "	想要買一個嗎 ? 」
and that's how most of us communicate .	這就是我們大多數人溝通 。

here's the best part: none of what i'm telling you is my opinion .	這是最好的部分:沒有我告訴你們的是我的選項 。

not psychology , biology .	不是心理學、生物學 。
if you look at a crosssection of the human brain , looking from the top down , what you see is the human brain is actually broken into three major components that correlate perfectly with the golden circle .	如果你仔細觀察人類大腦的雲朵 , 從頂端的角度來看 , 你看到的是人類大腦其實被破壞了三種主要的元件 。
our newest brain , our homo sapien brain , our neocortex , corresponds with the " what " level .	我們的新腦袋 , 我們的鄰居大腦、皮質、皮質、皮質、反應 。
the neocortex is responsible for all of our rational and analytical thought and language .	鄰居是對我們所有理性和分析的思想和語言 。
the middle two sections make up our limbic brains , and our limbic brains are responsible for all of our feelings , like trust and loyalty .	中間兩個選項會讓我們的肢體 , 我們的肢體是負責責責任 , 比如信任和孤獨 。
it's also responsible for all human behavior , all decisionmaking , and it has no capacity for language .	它也對所有人類行為的行為、所有決策、所有決策、所有決策 。
in other words , when we communicate from the outside in , yes , people can understand vast amounts of complicated information like features and benefits and facts and figures .	換句話說 , 當我們從外面溝通 , 是的 , 人們可以了解大量複雜的資訊 , 比如特徵和利潤和數字 。
it just doesn't drive behavior .	它不只是駕駛行為 。
when we can communicate from the inside out , we're talking directly to the part of the brain that controls behavior , and then we allow people to rationalize it with the tangible things we say and do .	當我們從內部溝通時 , 我們會直接和控制行為的一部分 , 我們允許人們對此行為的一部分 , 然後我們允許人們和做連結 。
this is where gut decisions come from .	這就是猜測的決定來自哪裡 。
you know , sometimes you can give somebody all the facts and figures , and they say , " i know what all the facts and details say , but it just doesn't feel right . "	你知道嗎 , 有時候你可以給別人所有事實 , 他們說: 「 我知道所有事實和細節說 , 「 我知道所有事實和細節 」
